Recent Military and Political News from Fujian Province 72

Fuzhou Correspondence - Lin Zhong, commander of the 1st Brigade of the Marine Corps stationed in Fujian and commander of the provincial defense, resigned from his concurrent positions because he was responsible for the political change on January 6 this year. The general headquarters of the Marine Corps stationed in Fujian transferred him to a senior advisor, and promoted Jin Zhenzhong, commander of the 1st Regiment of the brigade, to brigade commander, and Liu Gangde, commander of the 3rd Battalion of the 2nd Regiment, to regimental commander. All of this has been recorded in this newspaper. According to investigation, in addition to Lin Zhong, other naval generals involved in the January 6 political change include Sa Fuchou, commander of the Fujian Port Fortress, and Yu Bangyan, commander of the Ningfu Garrison. Now Sa Fuchou has also resigned, and the Marine Corps headquarters has approved the appointment of Mao Zhencai, chief of the headquarters' staff office, to succeed him. Sa was transferred to an advisor. Yu Bangyan has not yet made any expression as of the most recent time. After Lin and Sa left office, they both secretly lived at home. They did not take up the positions of advisor or counselor. Lin also plans to travel to Taiwan in the next few days. However, recently, there have been rumors that Chen Jiliang, the commander-in-chief of the Marine Corps, has also been very passive since Lin and Sa left. He has indicated that he intends to resign to Yang Shuzhuang. The chiefs of the various departments of the headquarters and the battalion commanders of the 1st Brigade said that Yang Shuzhuang has not been able to return to Fujian during this military period, and the affairs of Fujian province all depend on Chen. If Chen resigns again, no one in the naval agencies and troops in Fujian will be in charge, and actions will inevitably be chaotic. Therefore, they jointly retained him, saying that if Chen is determined to resign, they will all resign together. However, this statement has not been realized. Chen is still going to the headquarters every day as usual to work. Jin Zhenzhong also arrived in the province from Sandu Defense a few days ago and took office at the brigade headquarters in Majiang on the 2nd of this month.

Of the current members of the provincial government, Chen Peikun, Jiang Pingfan, and Lin Jinan, three people were previously appointed by the National Government. Chen Peikun was appointed as the acting chairman of the provincial government and concurrently acting director of the civil affairs and finance departments. Jiang Pingfan was acting director of the construction department, and Lin Jinan was acting director of the education department, temporarily maintaining the transitional period. Now Jiang and Lin have taken office successively, but Chen Peikun has repeatedly declined to take office, but still goes to the government office as usual. It is now becoming increasingly difficult to deal with civil and financial affairs, and he is extremely distressed. He telegraphed Yang Shuzhuang the other day, asking to be dismissed from his original position as a member of the committee and planned to go away for recuperation. Yang said that because he was unable to return to Fujian for a while, he relied entirely on Chen to preside over the affairs of the province and could not allow him to leave. He has replied by telegram to comfort him. However, Chen's attitude is still very passive. (July 2)

The Fujian Army Attacks Commander Lu 73

A Fuzhou dispatch reports that after the battle of Baisha Ridge, Commander Lu's troops retreated beyond Baisha, and Commander Liu's forces are about to converge. Supervising Commander Fang Shengtao is advancing. Furthermore, Chen Wenlin has twice flown airplanes to Youxikou and Damuxi to drop bombs, all of which hit their targets. The work of cutting trees, dredging moats, and building fortresses in key areas in the northwest is also proceeding steadily. The requisitioned automobiles continue to shuttle back and forth day and night without stopping. On June 30th, Liu Heding again traveled by car to Hongshan Bridge, where he transferred to a steamboat to go to the arsenal and then to the front line in the area of Pulidongkou for inspection. On the morning of the 1st of this month, at 4:00 AM, he again led officers and more than thirty horses to inspect the area between the Big and Small North Ridges outside the North Gate. He returned to the headquarters via the West Gate at around 10:00 AM. More than a thousand northwest prisoners transported from Shanghai have been undergoing training and replenishment in recent days.

True Situation of the Western Fujian Militia Suppressing Communists 74

Recapturing Longyan and Bangyang

A Xiamen dispatch from the 4th reports that in western Fujian, communist bandits, led by Deng Zihui of the Longyan Soviet, gathered the First Red Guard Team under Deng Gangyi and the Second Team under Fu Bocui, planning to assist Wu Zhonghe's communist forces under Zhu De in Shanghang to harass Guangdong. They repeatedly attacked Dapu but were repelled by the Guangdong army, suffering heavy losses. They then recruited and replenished forces in Yongding. As a result, the communist forces in the Longyan area are very weak, with only a small number of untrained soldiers from various villages left to guard the counties of western Fujian. Since the local militias in western Fujian have been reorganized and replenished, they have launched attacks on the communist bandits. On the 18th of last month, they recaptured Longyan County. Furthermore, the Zhongmin Militia recaptured Bangyang, Pingtou, and Tiandi on the 23rd. However, the communist disaster in western Fujian has been going on for a long time, and the telegraph lines have all been cut, with bandits everywhere and traffic blocked. As a result, the true situation is difficult to ascertain. One report says that the militia withdrew from Yan City on the 20th due to being isolated, but this has not been confirmed by official reports. Now, we have received a telegram from western Fujian about suppressing bandits, detailing the recapture of Longyan and Bangyang. We are recording the original telegram as follows:

(1) Liu Liebo, Head of the Yanshi Militia, telegram to Lin, Magistrate of Longyan: "Communist bandits are rampant, and the people of Yan are not at peace. Today, my troops departed from Subang to Yanshi to suppress the communist bandits. Our army attacked the enemy at dawn. More than 500 enemy rebels relied on dangerous terrain to resist stubbornly. After our army advanced bravely, the enemy could not withstand and fled in disarray towards Dongping Pass. In this battle, about 70 to 80 enemy soldiers were killed, more than 50 rifles were seized, and more than 20 enemy soldiers were captured. In addition to dispatching teams to search and pursue, this is reported to you and please forward to the superiors to quickly allocate ammunition to facilitate military operations." "Another telegram" Today, Zhi led more than 300 troops to depart from Yanshi and advance towards Yan City. The vanguard met the enemy at Dongping Pass and exchanged fire. Our army charged forward, and the enemy began to collapse. The enemy rebels employed many tricks and laid many ambushes along the way. Fortunately, our army was familiar with the terrain and attacked step by step, and were not trapped. At 2:00 PM, the enemy collapsed towards Longmen, and our army occupied Yan City. In this battle, about 50 to 60 enemy soldiers were killed, and more than 20 rifles and many military items were seized. However, my troops have fought the enemy repeatedly, and ammunition is very scarce, with each soldier having less than ten rounds. Although Yan City has been obtained, the enemy rebels are stirring up trouble on all sides. My troops are weak and cannot hold out for long. I am forced to telegraph to you, my lord, requesting you to send troops to reinforce and provide ammunition to boost morale and solidify our defense. I await your orders with trepidation."

(2) Magistrate of Longyan's reply to Head of the Liu Militia (titles omitted): "I have received your telegram. Your militia has braved the summer heat and launched attacks to suppress the communist bandits, winning many victories and capturing many prisoners, which has deterred the bandits in the city. Your martial labor is worthy of admiration. After receiving the news, this magistrate immediately telegraphed the Fujian Bandit Suppression Headquarters and the Provincial Government, and also discussed with the stationed army and the First Security Detachment to attack Yangbang and advance towards the county seat, and informed the Longtan and Fushi militias to launch guerrilla attacks towards Kanshi and Tiandi as reinforcements. Yangbang, Lantian, Shanpingtou and other places have been recaptured one after another, and are now advancing towards the Makeng area. The food for the officers and soldiers of the troops and the first district militia has been prepared and maintained nearby. As for the lack of ammunition, I have telegraphed the Provincial Government, the Fujian Bandit Suppression Headquarters, and General Sa to provide assistance. I hope you will continue to report the situation there by telegram to Magistrate Lin Kan Yin."

(3) The First Security Detachment reports the capture of Yangbang in a telegram: "Our Guo Battalion arrived in Yang on a certain day and went to the front to observe the situation for several days. Today, we attacked Yangbang together. Our Guo Battalion was responsible for the right wing, and our engineering battalion was responsible for the left wing. Our troops and the militias of various villages surrounded from the rear. We departed at 6:00 AM. The bandits were divided, half defending the towers stubbornly, and half relying on the mountains for support. After our army arrived, we fired seven and five shells at the Keto Tower, hitting four shells. More than ten mortar shells were fired, most of which also hit. At 10:00 AM, we broke through the tower and the bandits fled behind the mountain. We immediately divided our forces to pursue them. There were still two towers where the bandits were resisting stubbornly. Our army braved death and charged to the front of the tower, destroyed the gate, and the entire tower burned, and the bandits were burned to death. We heard their cries, which were estimated to be about thirty bandits inside. Our troops surrounded from the rear and engaged in fierce fighting with the bandits in Lixing Mountain. The bandits could not withstand and collapsed to the rear. Our troops followed and pursued them, and the bandits stationed in Tiandi, Shanpingtou, Lantian, Shimenlu and other places came to reinforce separately. Our troops fought them separately. After about an hour, the bandits suffered dozens of casualties and collapsed to the rear. Our troops pursued them to Shanpingtou, and another group pursued them to Lantian. These two places were also recovered one after another." End of telegram.

Huludao Groundbreaking Ceremony 75

A Shenyang dispatch reports that the Huludao Port Construction Groundbreaking Ceremony was held on July 2nd. Chinese and foreign guests attending the ceremony traveled by special train on the Beining Railway, departing from Shenyang at 11:30 PM on the 1st and arriving in Huludao the next morning. This was the first train, divided into consular, transportation, commercial, education, and reporter sections. The second train was for Zhang Xueliang and representatives from various parties, as well as important military and political figures from Liaoning Province. Two archways with the words "Welcome" were erected at the Lianshan Station, which is only a stone's throw from Huludao. An airfield was also temporarily opened with two white airplanes and one yellow airplane parked there for the Huludao groundbreaking ceremony. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Hall Arrangement: One side of a building occupied by the Naval Police School was converted into a hall, with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen and party and national flags hanging in the center. The walls were decorated with congratulatory messages from various parties. A podium was set up at the head of the hall, and chairs were arranged for about a hundred people.

Meeting Proceedings: At the beginning of the meeting, five warships anchored outside the island landed all the sailors and played music. Airplanes from Lianshan circled in the sky to celebrate. The meeting started at 2:30 PM in the following order: (1) Playing music, (2) Paying the highest respect to the party and national flags and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, (3) The chairman respectfully reading Sun Yat-sen's will, (4) Three minutes of silence, (5) Holding the groundbreaking ceremony, (6) Admonishment by Commander Zhang of the Northeast Border Defense Army, (7) Admonishment by the Minister of Railways, (8) A representative of the Northeast Political Affairs Committee reading a congratulatory message, (9) Guests making speeches, (after the speeches, everyone went to see the dynamite blasting the mountain), (10) Taking photos, (11) Playing music, (12) Entertainment by naval maneuvers and martial arts performances, (13) Closing the meeting.

Chairman's Speech: (1) Introduction A. Introductory remarks and humble words, B. A brief overview of the first port construction, C. A brief overview of the second port construction, D. The content of this port construction, (2) Discussion A. Reasons for port construction (1) Questioning the competition with Dalian Port, considering the establishment of a naval and commercial base in the Northeast, and considering it as an outer treasury of Northeast wealth, (2) Reasons: The environment favors and the people support it, taking the lead in international wharf construction, and connecting land and sea. B. Addressing the concerns of various parties, dispelling doubts about international intervention, dispelling doubts about the independent operation of the Beining Railway, dispelling doubts about insufficient funds, and dispelling doubts about Dutch contractors. (3) Conclusion A. The plan for this port (1) Scientific port construction (2) Economical port management organization (3) Civilized port administration facilities (4) International commercial operation B. Contributions to the future of this port C. Hope for support from all parties (1) The national government (2) The international community (3) Public opinion (4) The Dutch company (5) Colleagues at this port D. Closing remarks briefly stating that the presence of leaders, representatives and guests from all sides, despite the arduous journey and the summer heat, has expanded the meaning and value of this ceremony. On behalf of this port, I would like to express my heartfelt thanks. This project is unprecedented in China in the past ten years, and is worthy of the recognition and celebration of the people of the whole country. Therefore, this ceremony is not only a ritual that this port itself should have, but at the very least, it is also a memorable event worthy of the entire Chinese nation. I am very grateful to Minister Sun of the Ministry of Railways for his enthusiastic leadership in this port construction, and grateful to the central government for resolutely approving the port construction contract, and grateful to Mr. Hughes, the British engineer who initially selected Huludao Port, for the achievements of today. I have mediocre talents and dared not shoulder this important task, but I have been forced to do my best due to my duties. Fortunately, the entire project will still take five or six years, and perhaps outstanding talents will emerge to manage it in the future. I am also happy to fulfill my national duty by making a slight effort at the beginning of this project. (To be continued)

Ministry of Justice 76

The Judicial Officers Training Institute Continues to Recruit Students

The first class of students of the Judicial Officers Training Institute of the Ministry of Justice has graduated and has been submitted to the Judicial Yuan for approval to continue operation. The Institute has now determined the application dates for this session and will use Nanjing, Peiping, and Guangzhou as examination locations to recruit students. The abridged student recruitment guidelines are listed below: (1) Enrollment: 200 students (2) Graduation Period: One and a half years (3) Eligibility: Any member of the Kuomintang (Chinese Nationalist Party) who has graduated from a recognized national, public or private specialized school above with three or more years of study in law or political science and has a diploma, or any non-Kuomintang member who has the aforementioned diploma and has no counter-revolutionary activities and is willing to join the Party, may apply for the examination. (4) Order and Subjects of the Examination: (A) Preliminary Examination (B) Retest Those who pass the preliminary examination may take the retest. Those who pass the retest will be admitted to the institute for study. Preliminary Examination Subjects: (1) Party Principles and Program (2) Chinese (3) General Theory of Law Retest Written Examination Subjects: (1) Civil Law (2) Criminal Law (3) Civil Procedure Law (4) Criminal Procedure Law (5) Public International Law (6) Private International Law (7) Administrative Law Retest Oral Examination Subjects: (1) Civil Law (2) Criminal Law (3) Civil Procedure Law (4) Criminal Procedure Law (5) Application Locations: Capital (Nanjing): Ministry of Judicial Administration Guangzhou: Guangdong Higher Court Peiping: Second Branch of the Hebei Higher Court (6) Application Dates: From July 10th to August 15th of this year (7) Application Procedures: Applicants must submit two recent 4-inch half-length photos, documents proving their qualifications, Party membership card, and an application fee of two yuan (the application fee will not be refunded regardless of whether the applicant is admitted or not). (8) Graduation Benefits: After graduation, students will be assigned by the Ministry of Justice to fill vacancies as probationary investigators or prosecutors, and those who have studied elective courses at the Institute will be given priority in filling vacancies and receiving promotions.

Guangdong Public Sports Ground Construction Progresses 77

Construction Cost of 150,000 to be Appropriated by the Provincial Government in Installments

Preparatory Committee Established to Manage Implementation

Guangzhou Dispatch: The lack of a public sports ground in Guangdong Province has long been a regret for the sports community. Recently, Guangdong athletes at the Far Eastern Games, feeling the rapid progress of international sports, felt that the province must catch up quickly. Those in charge of education and sports experts believe that the construction of a public sports ground is imperative. It has been suggested for several years and resolved to build a public sports ground in Guangdong Province.

Page 9

Summary of Important News 78

To reclaim the wasteland of the East Parade Ground that has been sold by the government to merchants and civilians by paying for it. In addition, a preparatory committee for the public sports ground was established, and Xu Chongqing, Jin Zencheng, Lin Yungai, Chen Ce, Qiu Jixiang and other nine people were appointed as preparatory committee members. This matter was interrupted for a long time due to political and military influences. The committee members recently felt the urgency of promoting sports in eastern Guangdong and brought up the old matter again. A meeting was specially convened by the committee on the first of this month to discuss and decide on specific methods for construction of the sports ground. The results of the meeting that day were: (1) Land Acquisition Methods: (A) Determining the land to be acquired: The committee proposed to acquire a plot of land totaling approximately 9,645 Hua Jing and 20 square feet. (B) Establishing Boundaries: According to the original blueprint of the Department of Finance, a red line will be used as the boundary line, and boundary stones will be erected every ten zhang. (C) Demolishing Old Buildings: The original police and guerrilla team headquarters, naval and army comrades association, and police station within the grounds will all be notified by the provincial government to relocate separately, and the remaining private land will also be announced for acquisition. (D) Requesting Allocation of Funds: The provincial government originally planned to allocate 150,000 yuan for the construction of the sports ground. It is now proposed to request the allocation of 30,000 yuan for the first month starting in May, and 20,000 yuan for each month thereafter. (2) Hiring an engineer to draft architectural drawings for the sports ground. (3) Drafting the General Outline of the Committee Organization: The draft has been prepared as follows: Article 1: This committee is established by the Guangdong Provincial Government to supervise the construction of the sports ground. Article 2: This committee is composed of the following personnel: All committee members are volunteers and are appointed by the provincial government: the Director of the Department of Education, the Director of the Department of Construction, the Director of the Department of Finance, and six to eight experts. Article 3: This committee has three standing committee members, who are the Director of the Department of Education, the Director of the Department of Construction, and the Director of the Department of Finance. The standing committee members elect one person as chairman to preside over the affairs of the committee. Article 4: This committee holds a committee meeting once a week on a certain day and time each week. If there are special circumstances, the chairman will convene a temporary meeting. Article 5: This committee has an office to handle all affairs of the committee, with a general affairs director and a design director, each with several staff members, all of whom are selected or hired by the standing committee members. Article 6: The General Affairs Director is responsible for the accounting, general affairs, documents, equipment management of the sports ground, and other affairs of the committee. Article 7: The Design Director is responsible for the planning, supervision and management of the sports ground construction project. Article 8: Staff members assist the director in administrative tasks and are subject to his command and supervision. Article 9: The matters resolved by this committee are approved by the chairman and handed over to the staff for execution separately. Article 10: The general outline of this committee is approved and implemented by the provincial government. (July 1st)

Hangzhou Quick News 79

The Zhejiang Relief Association purchased 50,000 shi of cheap rice to provide relief to various counties. Since May, nearly 40,000 shi of cheap rice have been distributed to various counties. The remaining rice, approximately 10,000 shi, has been approved for distribution by the end of this month and will not be continued. This is because the new grain (early rice) in various counties will be harvested in early August. It is also reported that the cheap rice purchased this time was issued according to the purchase price, and the depreciation loss was quite large, requiring more than 100,000 yuan.

The Department of Construction found that construction projects in the southern part of the province were relatively few, so it organized an inspection team, hiring experts or assigning professionals from affiliated agencies to serve as inspectors. The inspection area is divided into three zones: the Oujiang River Basin as the first zone, the coastal counties as the second zone, and the upper reaches of the Qiantang River as the third zone. The inspection items are transportation, agriculture, geology, mining, water conservancy, and industry and commerce. The inspection period is tentatively set for three months.

The Provincial Highway Bureau submitted a request to the Department of Construction to establish a temporary repair shop, requiring approximately 23,000 yuan. It asked whether it could be approved to allocate funds for establishment and designated as a purely business organization. The proposal has been submitted to the Provincial Government Committee for deliberation and included in the budget for the 19th year. The Department of Finance has been notified to begin organization.

In May, Cantonese merchant Li Jiyun was kidnapped by bandits at the Yinma Bridge in Longjing, West Lake. The provincial government has issued an order to arrest and rescue the hostage, but two months have passed and the case has not been solved. Now, the Shanghai Cantonese Overseas Chinese Business Federation has telegraphed the provincial government again, requesting urgent arrest and resolution.

The Department of Finance found that the public expenditure budgets collected by various counties in Zhejiang Province were inconsistent due to their complexity. It has drafted a unified collection and expenditure method proposal and submitted it to the Provincial Government Committee for review and approval. It will be implemented after revision and passage. Local Dispatches 80

Jinshan

Robbed after being Forced to Lend: Yao Ahai, a farmer from Shanlu River West, north of the Kong Family Shrine, received a threatening letter from Tai Bao Ashu on the morning of May 23rd, sent by his subordinates Xi Daoming and Dai Kechang (more than a dozen households near the Kong Family Shrine received threatening letters on the same day). The letter clearly stated that they were borrowing 2,000 yuan in military pay and demanded that it be prepared within three days and paid at the Jiang Family Tea House in Henan, Wanchun Bridge. Ahai could not raise the money in time and failed to comply with the request. On the 30th, those people came again with many people to demand payment, all wearing box cannons and carrying several boxes of kerosene, claiming that if the money was not paid, they would burn down the house. Ahai was terrified and begged repeatedly, and finally agreed to pay 800 yuan to settle the matter. Unexpectedly, not long after, on the night of the 2nd of this month, three bandit ships came with more than 20 bandits, all carrying guns and weapons. They rushed in and tied up the family members one by one, severely tortured and beat them, and forced them to hand over silver dollars. Ahai was the most seriously injured and his life was in danger. Dozens of shi of soybeans, wheat, rapeseed, etc., as well as silver dollars, ornaments, clothes, quilts, and all utensils were robbed, causing great losses. Then they boarded the ship fully loaded and left.

Songjiang

Change of Funding for the County Labor and Agricultural Farm: The funding for the county labor farm has been stagnant since the budget was revised last year. Now that the 19th year has begun, the funding for the farm should be discussed and decided to maintain it. At the county administrative meeting the other day, there were discussions on the funding for the county labor farm and agricultural farm. Should the existing 3,040 yuan of county tax funding for the county labor farm, 846 yuan for the former agricultural farm nursery, and 440 yuan for the former farmers' association be stopped uniformly according to the order of the department, and all funding for the labor farm and agricultural farm be changed to be paid from the special construction fund and the agricultural improvement mu loss item, so as to free up 4,326 yuan of county tax to make up for the insufficient expenditure of other county funds? The discussion resulted in a resolution that the construction bureau's funding that originally had provincial subsidies had been ordered to stop, and the county's revenue from the county construction fee was also insufficient to allocate. The funding for the county labor farm should be reduced in scope and still subsidized by 100 yuan per month under the county tax item to maintain it. The original allocation of 1,286 yuan for the agricultural farm under the county tax item should be stopped entirely. The funding for the farm should be paid from the agricultural improvement mu loss item in accordance with the order of the department. The county will compile a transformation budget and submit it to the county for compilation.

Hunan Refugees Leave Song Today: The other day, approximately 300 Hunanese refugees came to Song from Xinqiao along the railway and stayed in the Huayang Bridge area outside the East Gate, occupying places such as Ziyang Palace and Dongchan Temple. The so-called refugee leaders were all dressed in luxurious clothes and used expensive items. Huayang Town Chief Xu Chunbo gathered 40 to 50 yuan and 3 shi of rice to provide food, but it was still not enough to satisfy their desires. Town Chief Xu personally requested the county government to send a police team to drive them away. This morning, they left Song on foot towards Jiashan.

Fengxian

Detailed Account of the Solved Kidnapping Case: Details of the case in which Yang Shusen, the captain of the second police squad of the county, solved the kidnapping case and rescued the hostages. Captain Yang of the squad was investigating very carefully since the kidnapping case of the Lu family in Zhuangxing occurred. On the 3rd of this month, a scout reported that the house of Su Agui at No. 29, Zhugang Dongtan, four li away from the town, had seen many pieces of washed children's clothes every morning. When asked, the neighbors said that the house had no children. Thinking that traces could be found, he led 20 police officers at 3:30 AM that night, braving the rain to rush to the location. He first surrounded the residence, and then ordered the squad leader wearing a steel wire vest and six police officers to rush into the inner bedroom. The bandit Wang Ahe, who was guarding the hostages, had already heard the noise and got up to resist with a gun. Fortunately, the squad leader was quick and captured him. At the same time, the other two bandits were also captured by the police one after another, and no one escaped. All five hostages were hidden in the side room in the east, in the pit house firewood room. Captain Yang personally rescued them and escorted them to Zhuangxing before dawn on the 4th, and then transferred them to the Nanhua Brigade headquarters to await interrogation. It is now known that the county magistrate Shen has sent Ding Zhiyan from the brigade to hold a preliminary hearing yesterday afternoon. Su Agui confessed that he was 22 years old and a native of the county. Last month, he and 17 others formed a partnership, called for two ships, had five handguns, went to Liuzhi Town, Kunshan County to kidnap two Zhou family members, and then kidnapped three Chen family members in Zhangpu Town. Ten days ago, they secretly transported them to the countryside and hid them. He just returned from Shanghai yesterday and was completely unprepared. Wang A'er (the monk), who was watching the ticket, confessed that he lived in Nanhui and worked in a yarn factory in Caojiadu, Shanghai. This time, Su Agui and Su A'mei called him on the first day of this month, gave him a handgun to watch the tickets. He heard that the old class of Agui belonged to Cao Amu of Caoging. Shen Youdi confessed that he lived in Xuejiaqiao Town, Qingpu, met Su and others in Yaodabang, and invited him to come and watch the three little tickets. It was agreed that he would be paid 100 yuan for the job. As for the two tickets of the Zhou family, they were watched by Wang Ahe. There was also a female bandit, who initially confessed to He Aizhen, but later changed her name to Xu A'mei. Her words were disjointed. She said that she was from Songjiang and was lured by Su Agui. After interrogating the hostages, Zhou Jinqing confessed that he lived in the countryside of Liuzhi Town, Kunshan County, was 68 years old, and his mailing address was at Hongfu Teagarden in the town. His family was not rich and made a living by farming. He had only one son named Yongkang. This time, the bandits kidnapped his grandson Wenwei. Because he resisted desperately, he was kidnapped here together for about ten days. The bandits told him that his family had entrusted someone to negotiate the price, but no agreement had been reached. Chen Kechang, Chen Keliang, and Chen Keyan confessed that they lived in Zhangpu Town, Kunshan County, about ten li away from the city, and were brothers of the same clan. They were fourteen or nine years old. Their father was named Chen Zhengbao and made a living by farming. When they were kidnapped, the bandits used handguns to force them to board the ship. At first, they were hidden in the bow of the ship and were not allowed to make any noise or visit. They shook for four or five days before arriving at Su's house and were imprisoned in the bedroom in the back house for ten days. Usually the bandits came and went a lot, and at night they were accompanied by bandits for surveillance. He still remembered that the Su bandit said when he went to Shanghai a few days ago that if his family did not redeem them, he would tear up the ticket, and ordered me to take off my clothes and be beaten. Now, please notify Kong Dayuan Nanhua store in Zhangpu Town to inform their family to come and collect them. After interrogation, Ding, the captain of the brigade, in addition to detaining the three bandits Su, Wang, and Shen in the county, asked the Kunshan County Government and each family to prepare documentary evidence to await identification and return. As for the female bandit, after an interrogation, it was found that she had nothing to do with the kidnapping case and could have been released. However, because her confessions were inconsistent, the Songjiang County Government was asked to investigate the woman's family before verifying the facts. Captain Yang was commended by County Magistrate Shen Qingkang for solving the major case repeatedly and for his hard work.

Wuxi 81

Record of Interrogation in the Gunning Down of Tan Qixuan Case: Tan Qixuan, the former head of the Beishang Township Administrative Bureau in Xiyi, was tragically shot and killed by bandits on April 1st of last year. Subsequently, the county authorities arrested Bao Dayuan, Lü Genhu, Guo Asi, Guo Ada, and Sun Junxi, the former head of the county party headquarters' propaganda department, and Lü Shiqiao, a clerk, who were all involved in the case. They were interrogated and detained by the county. A few days ago, police officers were dispatched to the township to arrest Chen Yangong and Yu Yaocheng, two people related to the case, and brought them to the county. Tang Yiqin, a member of the committee for clearing accumulated cases, opened a court session and summoned them for interrogation. Chen Yangong was found to be unrelated and was released on bail in court. Yesterday afternoon, at about 1 p.m., Tan Zhongying (Tan Qixuan's father), the plaintiff, and Pu Xiehan, a witness, were summoned, and the defendants in custody were brought in for questioning. First, Tan Zhongying testified, "My son Qixuan went out with Lü Shiqiao on April 1st to collect donations. After lunch at Lü's house, he said goodbye and returned.

On the way, he was shot by bandits with a pistol.

After falling to the ground, he was carried to the administrative bureau, where he told me, 'I fell into Lü Shiqiao's trap.' He also said that there were four bandits, and he only recognized Bao Dayuan," and then he was sent to the hospital by boat, but he died before he could be rescued. Next, Bao Dayuan, Lü Genhu, Guo Asi, and Zhu Ada were interrogated. Except for Bao Dayuan, who still claimed that after the meeting in Songshan, Lü Shiqiao met him on the road and ordered him to shoot and kill Tan Qixuan, which he refused to do, the others were vague and unwilling to tell the truth. Next, Sun Junxi testified that he had applied to the High Court for a change of jurisdiction and therefore refused to make a statement. Next, Lü Shiqiao testified that he and Qixuan had always been on good terms and that he had no intention of seizing his position as director or murdering him. Then, the witness Pu Xiehan was questioned. Next, Yu Yaocheng testified that he was detained in the detention center for a case when Tan Qixuan was killed, so he did not know anything about it. After the interrogation, Tan Zhongying and Pu Xiehan were ordered to return home, and Yu Yaocheng was released on bail. Bao Dayuan, Lü Shiqiao, Sun Junxi, Lü Genhu, Guo Asi, Zhu Ada, and others were all returned to custody to await further interrogation and judgment.

Chen Lunkui Declared Not Guilty: Chen Lunkui, a native of Anzhen, Xiyi, once served as an instructor in the Huaixia urban district party headquarters in the 16th year of the Republic of China. Because of his upright words and deeds, he aroused jealousy from certain parties and was falsely accused of being a counter-revolutionary suspect. He was wanted by the authorities. At the end of last year, Chen Lunkui was arrested in Rugao by the rural cleanup bureau and sent to the Suzhou High Court for trial. Recently, after investigation by the Procuratorate of the High Court, it was confirmed that there was no suspicion of counter-revolution, and it was decided not to prosecute him and release him in court. He has already returned to Xiyi.

Pheasant Prostitutes Detained for Interrogation: More than ten houses along the city wall outside the Guangfu Gate of Xiyi are inhabited by wild chickens (i.e., pheasant prostitutes). It is common to see them soliciting customers along the way. The Second Public Security Branch is nearby, but it has not been heard that they have been cracked down on. Recently, a large number of people from other places have come to the town, and some of them spend all day there for pleasure, which is related to the local public order. County Magistrate Sun Zuji and Public Security Bureau Chief Huang Zhenbai were aware of this situation and, on the afternoon of the 5th, ordered Sun Rongding, the chief of the Second Public Security Branch in charge, to send police officers to arrest ten people, including the old pimp Luo Fagen, the pheasant prostitutes Wang Lanzhen, Luo Pengshi, Zhu Jinmei, Shi Qiaoyun, Jin'e, Wang Yuehong, and Yu Xiaomei, Zhu Xiaomei. They were taken to the County Public Security Bureau to await orders.

Jiangyin

False Accusation Against the Head of the Defense Corps: County Magistrate Li Leng received an express letter from Changzhou on June 6th, sent by Ligang Township, in which Wang Jie, who gave his name, filed a complaint accusing Ling Hesheng, the head of the Ding Taosha Defense Corps, and squad leader Huan Da of colluding with bandits north of the Yangtze River. County Magistrate Li then ordered Cao Weihan, the chief of the Houmei Sixth Public Security Branch, to investigate. It turned out that there was no such person as the plaintiff Wang Jie, and Ling Hesheng and others had no suspicion of colluding with bandits. The case was reported to the general bureau and then to the county for handling. On the same day, Corps Leader Ling also went to the county to explain the situation. The clerk Shen Jizhou met him and, since there was no relation to the case, ordered him to return.

Bureau Chief Slaps Subordinate, Who Commits Suicide Out of Resentment: Yang Xueying, the chief of the Second Public Security Branch of Houtang, has been incompatible with the patrol officers since taking office due to his stubborn personality. The other day, he slapped the patrol officer Li Ali six three times over a trivial matter. Li committed suicide out of resentment. Yesterday (the 5th), his younger brother filed a complaint with the county government accusing Chief Yang of coercion and requesting that someone be sent to the countryside to conduct an autopsy. After County Magistrate Li received the complaint, he immediately sent judicial secretary Lu Baoguang and coroner Cao to the countryside to conduct an autopsy.

Opening of Rice Sales to Relieve the Poor: The county government held a meeting on maintaining food supplies for the people on the 5th and resolved: (1) The deficit of 20,000 yuan for grain reserves must be paid by 9 a.m. on the 10th by Director Shen of the Finance Bureau and the director of the Xia Kuanshan Office, who shall be fully responsible for this. (2) The price of rice sold should be 2 yuan per picul. (3) The date for the opening of rice sales in urban and rural areas will be the 20th. (4) Donations from each district must be submitted to the association before July 20th.

The Truth of the Zhu Tingyu Case Is Difficult to Ascertain: On the 30th of last month, the investigation team arrested Zhu Tingyu, Zhu Ronggui, Xiao Yunzhang, and three other suspicious persons in the Lu Family Garden in the city. After interrogation by the county bureau, no definite confession was obtained. Yesterday (the 5th), Wu Shanbao, who was sent to Shanghai by the investigation team to investigate, returned to Cheng and reported that there was no Yufeng Lumber Company or Hong Baosheng in Xiaojiadu, and no Kang Shuitian in Huile Lane. The telegram from Zhu Tingyu, Zhu Kongwen, has denied sending a letter, which shows that Zhu and others are definitely not good people. After seeing the report in the newspaper, the Shanghai General Patrol House sent Chief Inspector Feng Shuofu of the General Investigation Department to Cheng yesterday to investigate whether Zhu Tingyu and others were related to the tragic murder of seven lives in the Guo residence on Avenue Edward VII. After confirming that there was no connection, he returned to Shanghai to report. However, the nature of Zhu Tingyu's crimes is now being investigated in detail by the investigation team, which has been transferred to the judiciary.

Banditry Rampant at the Junction of Tonghai: In recent days, a large number of bandits have gathered and rioted in the Erzhen area at the junction of Nantong and Haimen counties, killing defense corps police officers and forcing villagers to join the pseudo-Red Army. The Anti-Bandit Command Headquarters of the Nine Counties in the North has mobilized a large detachment of Yu Shimei's troops to suppress them. The Trial of the Tragic Death of the Owner of the Automobile Company: Jiang Chuntang, the owner of the Lu Shun Automobile Company in the new market south of the city, was beaten to death by the county police team due to a conflict over the sealing of hired vehicles. The defendants Liang Qinghai and Wang Hongchen gave very cunning confessions. Police Officers Oppose Misappropriation of Public Security Land Tax: The police officers of the entire county of Tongyi unanimously opposed the allocation and use of the collected public security land tax for other agencies and requested the County Political Affairs Conference to reconsider and correct the situation so that no agency could misappropriate the funds. Rugao

Memorial Service for Fallen Police Officers in Shizhuang: Yesterday, all sectors of Shizhuang held a memorial service at Shizhuang Elementary School to commemorate the county police officers who died in Shizhuang. After the police public sacrifice, the team marched out and sent the memorial tablets of the martyrs to the City God Temple for placement. Along the way, they shouted slogans. Guests freely donated 400 yuan, and it was decided to provide 200 yuan in consolation to the family of squad leader Liu Han and 100 yuan to the police officers, which have now been distributed to their families.

Frequent Bandit Disasters in the Southwest: Zhang Wansheng, a resident of Guandi Temple in Hedong Township, opened a butcher shop. Last night, forty or fifty bandits came and severely beat his wife, killing her by hitting her head with a box cannon. His younger brother, Wanxuan, was dragged out and killed with knives, sticks, and gunshots. Cheng Jiasheng, who lived nearby and collected eggs, and Zhang Laocha of Shaojia Village, who worked as a matchmaker, were both suspected of being spies by the bandits and shot to death. Zhenjiang

Collapse of the Liuyi Riverbank Injures People: Liuyi (i.e., Jiaxing Bridge) on the opposite bank of Zhenjiang is an important junction for ferries and automobiles. Yesterday afternoon at 1 p.m., the Puji Ferry was carrying dozens of passengers and was sailing across the river, heading straight for the north bank. When it was about ten feet away from the dock, the riverbank suddenly collapsed with a loud noise. A section of the bank two feet wide and ten feet long collapsed, and the waves rose high, overtopping the ship's mast and causing the Puji Ferry to capsize and lie sideways in the river. The bow of the ship had already sunk, and the situation was extremely dangerous. Fortunately, the driver had foresight and used full reverse gear to turn the ship upright. However, seven or eight passengers standing by the side of the ship preparing to disembark were swept away by the waves, and Wang Xiaokouzi, the ship's tea attendant, also disappeared at the same time. The seats in the ship's large dining room were broken, the decorations were damaged, and the railings on the second floor deck were broken and destroyed. It will require major repairs. After escaping danger, the ship limped back to the Liujiyuan Wharf and reported the incident to the manager's office. Automobile ferry services have also been suspended pending the restoration of the ship. Chief Zhu, the Jiaxing Bridge water police officer, is currently hiring people to salvage objects and asking people to claim them.

Gaoyou

Two Bandit Cases: The family of Chen Changshan, a farmer in Guangfeng Township under the county's jurisdiction, had a boy kidnapped by bandits last month. Due to the difficulty of raising a large sum of money, he has not been redeemed to this day. The night before last, five bandits armed with guns broke into his house and demanded that he quickly prepare 5,000 yuan to redeem the boy, threatening to tear up the ticket if he was late. After saying this, they fired their guns and left. The night before last, seven or eight bandits suddenly came to the Three Hundred and Sixth Village under the county's jurisdiction and searched every house, and no one was spared. It is said that the losses were huge.

Tragic News Amidst Rising Rice Prices: A Jin woman in Jinjia Township under the county's jurisdiction has been widowed for many years. She has elderly parents-in-law above her and five children below. The entire family of eight depends on meager property for a living. However, in recent times, rice and firewood have become increasingly expensive, and life has become increasingly difficult. The Jin woman suddenly had a pessimistic thought and went to a noodle shop to buy several catties of flour. She secretly mixed arsenic into the flour and made cakes, which they ate together. After a while, they all died from the poison. It is indeed tragic.

Jiaxing

Expansion of the Hezhou Security Team: Jiang Zhaozhou, the battalion commander of the Third Battalion of the Seventh Regiment of the Hezhou Security Team, has now received orders from his superiors to expand into a four-company system. The original Seventh and Ninth Companies of the Third Battalion have been incorporated into the First Battalion. However, the Eighth Company has been changed to the Tenth Company of the Third Battalion. The remaining Ninth, Eleventh, and Twelfth Companies have been reassigned from the directly subordinate companies of the First Battalion and the regimental headquarters. The reorganization has been completed. The Third Battalion headquarters and the Tenth Company under its jurisdiction are stationed at the Xuanmiao Temple in Jiaxing. The Ninth Company is stationed at the Jingyan Temple. The Eleventh Company has been sent to Jiashan to take over the defense. The Twelfth Company will be transferred from Hangzhou to Hezhou in the near future to strengthen the defense.

Problems with District Office Expenses: The expenses of the district offices in Jiaxing cannot be carried out due to the lack of funds. It is learned that the 15th County Political Affairs Conference has resolved to use two jiao per liang of the local surtax and three jiao per shi of the surtax on the Jin as compensation from the 19th year onwards. It is said that the matter has been submitted to the Civil and Financial Departments for approval and will be announced soon. However, the owners of various businesses believe that the surtax on the local compensation Jin has exceeded the positive number, and there have always been funds for handling autonomy. Now, instead of reclaiming the original autonomous items, five jiao is added to the land tax compensation Jin, which increases the burden on the people and is not in line with the intention of cherishing the people's difficulties. Therefore, they plan to jointly telegraph the province to request that the county be ordered to exempt the additional surtax and, on the one hand, recover the original district funds for distribution to benefit autonomy.

A Case of Murdering Her Husband Discovered in the Tanghui District: Zheng Aisheng, 30 years old, from Niaoqiao Village, Tanghui, west of the ferry crossing (i.e., across the river from the Tanghui Public Security Branch), has a wife named Shen Youlan who has been unfaithful by nature and has had an affair with Peng Xiaomei from Taizhou for many years. The neighbors all know about it. Because Zheng is there, it is very inconvenient. The other night, the adulterous couple took advantage of Zun's sound sleep and stabbed Zheng's throat and chest twice with a knife, killing him. The Tanghui Public Security Branch heard about it and immediately ordered the police to go to the scene for an inspection. Shen Youlan was arrested, but Peng Xiaomei had already fled without a trace. The matter was immediately reported to the local branch court for an autopsy. The autopsy revealed that the deceased had a knife wound on his chest and throat, and there were also toxic substances in his abdomen. The adulterous woman Shen Youlan has been taken back to the court for strict interrogation, and Peng Xiaomei, the adulterous man, is being strictly hunted down and brought to justice for interrogation.

(Resolution) It will be submitted for review and discussed at the next meeting.

Education News

Important News 82

Ministry of Education Stipulates the Length of Medical Studies

The Ministry of Education has stipulated the length of study and practice for the pre-medical and undergraduate programs of medical colleges. In addition to issuing notices and instructions to various universities and special municipalities, it has also ordered the education departments of various provinces to investigate medical education matters, which are of utmost importance. It is necessary to determine the study procedures to be followed. The ministry has now stipulated that students of university medical colleges must have a high school diploma before entering the two-year pre-medical program before entering the undergraduate program. This type of pre-medical program is managed by the university's college of science. This is an independent medical college or in special circumstances (such as the university does not have a college of science or the college of science and the medical college are far apart), its pre-medical program may be requested to be affiliated with other university colleges of science. When it is unavoidable, it may also be set up in the college. During the five years of undergraduate studies, there is one year of internship. All university medical colleges and independent medical colleges should follow these regulations. In addition to issuing notices and distributing them, it is hereby ordered that the relevant department forward this order to all provincial and private universities and independent medical colleges in the province for compliance.

Ministry of Education Moves Up Summer Office Hours

Various ministries and departments under the government, such as the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, have already moved up their office hours last week. During the summer vacation, the Ministry of Education has moved its ordinary office hours to 7 a.m. to 12 p.m. every day from the 7th. Although most of the staff rest in the afternoon, each department has people taking turns on duty. In case of urgent matters and meetings, they will still be handled at any time.

Students of University-Affiliated High Schools Must Not Be Exempt from Entrance Exams

The Ministry of Education has stipulated that graduates of university-affiliated high schools must not be exempt from examinations and directly enter their respective universities. In addition to issuing instructions to various universities, it has also notified the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities to investigate the abolition of preparatory courses in universities. When it is unavoidable, they are allowed to run affiliated senior high schools, which were originally established to help students enter higher education. However, after graduation, students must not be exempt from examinations and directly enter their respective universities. They must still be treated the same as other high school graduates, and go through the entrance examination to select the best candidates to ensure fairness and prevent abuse. In addition to issuing notices and distributing them, it is hereby ordered that the relevant department forward this order to all provincial and private universities in the province for compliance.

Zhejiang Province Schedules Examination for Local Education Administrators

The examination for local education administrators in Zhejiang Province was originally scheduled to be held in April. After the National Government issued an order promulgating the effective date of the examination law, the provincial government submitted the examination regulations for education administrators for review. The examination institute has now revised and approved the scheduled holding of the examination. The examination matters are recorded below: Qualifications: Any citizen of the Republic of China who is at least 25 years old and has one of the following qualifications: (1) Graduated from a university or independent college majoring in education and has a certificate. (2) Graduated from a normal university or higher normal school and has a certificate. (3) Graduated from a higher normal school elective course or a part one or two of the old-style normal school undergraduate program or a senior high school normal course and has a certificate and has served in an educational position for more than two years with documentary evidence. Examination procedure: (1) Qualification review (2) Physical examination (3) Written examination (4) Oral examination Examination subjects: (1) The Three Principles of the People, the Founding Strategy, the Founding Program, the History of the Chinese National Revolution (2) Chinese Education Principles, Educational Psychology, Current Education Laws and Regulations, Education Administration, Education Conditions in the Province, Education Statistics and Tests, Elementary School Teaching Methods, Elementary School Organization and Administration, Elementary School Training, Elementary School Teaching Materials and Curriculum The registration period is extended to July 25. A detailed resume, graduation certificate, and

Service certificate, and two recent 4-inch half-length photos must be submitted at the time of registration. The examination fee is two yuan. Examination period: August 1st for qualification review, August 11th for physical examination, August 14th to August 16th for written examination, August 19th for oral examination. Registration location: Zhejiang Education Institute, Pinghai Road, Hangzhou. Announcement: This time, only education bureau directors and county supervisors are allowed to take the examination. A letter with the regulations is available upon request.

Zhejiang Education Department Reorganizes Joint County Middle Schools

The joint county-run secondary schools in the former Jinhua, Wenzhou, and Taizhou prefectures in Zhejiang Province are mostly in financial straits and difficult to manage. Except for the former Jinhua County-run Bawai Women's Middle School, which has a board of directors responsible for maintaining operations and is achieving good results, the other joint schools in the former Wenzhou and Taizhou prefectures have found it particularly difficult to maintain operations because the board of directors has not yet been organized. In order to reorganize these schools, the Education Department issued orders to the counties yesterday, requiring them to follow the measures for establishing secondary schools in cities and counties during the summer vacation to organize a board of directors to assist and seek development.

Local 83

New Measures for Enrollment of Private Universities in Shanghai Municipal Area

Approved by the Ministry of Education and Implemented by the Municipal Education Bureau

Since the new academic year is about to begin, the Shanghai Special Municipal Education Bureau is concerned that the qualifications of new students admitted by various private universities in the city will vary, which will make teaching difficult and make it difficult to improve the university level. Therefore, it has drafted six provisional measures for the enrollment of new students by private universities in the Shanghai Special Municipal Area and submitted them to the Ministry of Education for approval. After receiving the submission, the Ministry of Education believed that the measures drafted by the bureau were well-intentioned, made slight revisions to the original measures, and ordered the bureau to comply with them. The following is a summary of the provisional measures: (1) When private universities in the Shanghai Special Municipal Area enroll new students, the committee's established plan shall be reported to the Municipal Education Bureau and forwarded to the Ministry of Education in advance. (2) When private universities hold entrance examinations for new students, the examination methods and procedures shall be reported to the Municipal Education Bureau and forwarded to the Ministry of Education in advance. (3) When private universities hold entrance examinations for new students, the Ministry of Education or the Municipal Education Bureau may send personnel to investigate at any time. (4) If private universities exempt new students from all or part of the examination subjects, the reasons for the exemption shall be reported to the Municipal Education Bureau and forwarded to the Ministry of Education for approval in advance. If necessary, inspections may be carried out at any time. (5) The Municipal Education Bureau shall check the graduation certificates of the applicants when private universities hold entrance examinations. If the applicants have graduation certificates from unaccredited university preparatory courses and senior high schools, or have no certificates, they shall be ordered to stop the examination. (6) If private universities do not comply with the above measures, the Municipal Education Bureau may submit a request to the Ministry of Education to impose penalties in accordance with Article 6 of the Private School Regulations.

County Education Bureau Plans to Establish a

Mass Education Experiment Zone

The Shanghai County Education Bureau is actively proceeding with the Mass Education Experiment Zone it is planning to establish. All the plans have been drafted and approved for implementation at a meeting. The plan is summarized as follows: (1) Name: The area is named the Shanghai County Mass Education Experiment Zone. (2) Purpose: The purpose of this zone is to experiment with socialized mass schools suitable for the conditions in this county and to implement the results of the experiments throughout the county. (3) Area: The mass education institutions run by the bureau, except for mass schools, are biased towards the west bank of the Huangpu River. For the sake of equal distribution of educational institutions, the zone should be located in Sanlin, Pudong. This matter has already been approved by the current Education Administrative Committee. However, if the entire Sanlin area is taken as the scope, the area is over 60 li in size, making it difficult to experiment with socialized mass schools. Therefore, one township in that autonomous region will be temporarily used as the area. Over the past month, the bureau has been in contact with the administrative authorities of the district several times, and it has been tentatively decided that Ruilong Township in the east of the district will be the area, and the Ruilong Temple in the township will be used as the temporary office. The east of the township is about one li away from Yangsi District in the special municipality, and six li away from Sanlin Town in the west. The transportation is convenient. The township has more than 100 households, and there is a trend of concentration. The residents are mostly engaged in agriculture, which is suitable for use as a mass education experiment zone. (4) Equipment: Since the purpose of this zone is to experiment with socialized mass schools suitable for the conditions in various parts of the county, if the selected area is not representative of the conditions in various parts of the county or is otherwise unsuitable as an experiment zone, it should be moved at any time. Therefore, all the equipment in the zone should be as simple as possible during the trial period, and it should be added after it is considered possible to continue the experiment. Moreover, during the preparation period, the forms of education needed by the masses are not yet known, and the living conditions of the masses are still unclear. If equipment is prematurely and presumptuously procured, it will be difficult to avoid the regret of cutting one's feet to fit the shoes. Therefore, the equipment in this zone must not be arbitrarily purchased during the trial period. At present, during the trial period, it is only necessary to rent three thatched houses and make some repairs to serve as the office for the staff of the zone and for trial use. As for the desks, chairs, and teaching aids needed by the mass school, they should also be purchased according to the urgency of the needs. (5) Staff: A. Staff Types: (1) Director-General (Concurrently held by the Director of the County Education Bureau or the Director of the Social Education Section, temporarily without pay. The zone's officer may be requested to serve as an agent at ordinary times.) (2) One officer for the Literacy Education Section, Investigation Section, and Readings Editing Section. (3) One officer for the Livelihood Education Section and Recreation Education Section. (4) One officer for the Political Education Section and Health Education Section. B. Staff Recruitment Standards: (1) General Standards: (1) High moral character, obedience to the Party. (2) Must have the spirit of researching and experimenting with mass education. (3) Must have a strong interest in rural life and the spirit of hard work and endurance. (4) Be kind and simple, able to approach the masses, and worthy of being a model for the masses. (2)

(1) The officer for the Literacy Education Section, Investigation Section, and Readings Editing Section must have in-depth research on education and considerable experience in reading material editing, social investigation, and editing. (2) The officer for the Livelihood Education and Recreation Education must have considerable experience and knowledge in agricultural science and experience in cooperative undertakings, and must have the skills to guide the masses in noble recreational methods. The officer for Political Education and Health Education must have considerable knowledge and experience in political education and health education. Clerical staff, accountants, and clerks will be concurrently held by the staff of each section and will not be hired separately for the time being. (6) Organization: Director-General of the Shanghai County Mass Education Experiment (1)) General Affairs Department: divided into three sections: document, affairs, and accounting. (2) Instruction Department: divided into seven sections: health, livelihood, household affairs, political, literacy, social interaction, and recreation education. (3) Research Department: divided into two sections: investigation and editing. (7) Phased Implementation: (1) Trial Period: Conduct social surveys, statistics, and planning and facility matters, and in accordance with the Mass Education Implementation Regulations promulgated by the Education Department, one mass school (i.e., classroom teaching) or one central tea garden may be tried first (tentatively for three months). (2) Implementation Period: Engage in research and experimentation on new theories and methods in mass education. (3) Implementation and Promotion Period: Continue to implement as in the previous period, but the results of the experiment must first be promoted in the entire Sanlin area, and then gradually promoted throughout the county. (8) Regulations of the Preparatory Committee: omitted.

Disturbance at Fudan Experimental Middle School

The issue of the director of Jiangwan Fudan Experimental Middle School has always been resolved by the general assembly of all faculty and staff of the school. At the end of this semester, the director of the school, Chen Wangdao, submitted his resignation. The general assembly decided to retain him and only allowed him to take leave, and elected three people for Chen Wangdao to designate one of them as an acting director. As a result, Li Baochen received the most votes with nineteen votes and was designated as the acting director. Afterwards,

many faculty and staff believed that it was a contempt for public opinion and a destruction of the spirit of the conference. Therefore, yesterday (July 6), they organized a school protection association and resolved on the spot to absolutely safeguard the resolutions of the faculty and staff conference, issued a declaration refusing to accept the illegal acting director's appointment letter, and many other important matters. They elected Kuai Shixun, Liu Zhixin, and Gui Yu Zhou as chairmen, and Di Xichen, Feng Lisan, Li Weinong, Jue Jiabin, Ma Shigang and others, nine people, to organize an executive committee to carry out all affairs.

Sports

Japanese Criticism of Our Country's Basketball Team Tactics 85

Enemy Opinions, May Our Team Members Pay Attention (Lao)

Bearing Hardship with Patience for Four Years

The basketball team representing our country at this Far Eastern Games was composed of first-class players from both the North and the South, and was known as an ever-victorious army. Therefore, it was believed that the championship of the Games would be ours. Unexpectedly, the result was beyond expectations and created a new Far Eastern record of four defeats in four games. In addition to the pain and anger of the Chinese people, they have spared no effort to study the reasons for the failure in preparation for our team to avenge its shame in the 10th Games. The criticisms of Mr. Xu and Mr. Lu in this newspaper are unique and have made great contributions to the basketball community in our country. The Japanese have a lot of harsh criticisms of our team. Here are two of them that have not been mentioned by the two gentlemen, which are translated for the reference of the Chinese people.

The Opinion of Li Xiangbai, Supervisor of the Basketball Team at Waseda University in Tokyo

The Chinese team's shooting, passing, and dribbling skills are all below those of the Japanese team, and their coordination is the least skilled and extremely chaotic. Their strong physique is their only advantage. In other words, they are just a team of talented players. The Chinese team's tactics are extremely clumsy and still in the simplest stage of basketball practice. Their most successful tactic is the vertical offense, that is, a forward goes to the middle and rushes into enemy territory to receive the pass from the rear and shoot. It is always the same and is very easy for the enemy to know and be watched by the enemy. There are no other strategies to replace it, which is why they were completely defeated.

Moreover, the Japanese team's guards, Ooba and Kobayashi, have genius skills in defending against this offensive method. Therefore, when the Chinese team used this tactic, except for Tang Baokun, who had one or two examples of success, or others who used their height to shoot under the basket or use long shots to gain cunning, they were almost unable to enter the Japanese basket. When the Japanese forwards retreated to take a defensive posture, it goes without saying that the Chinese team was exhausted and defeated.

The poor defense is not unique to the Chinese team. Japan and the Philippines are also like this. Relying on speed and talent, they pay attention to offense and do not care about defense. This is a chronic problem in China and the Philippines. When the five-man defensive method is not skillfully used, it can still be dealt with. Now, it is simply impossible not to be defeated. Comparing the strengths of the Japanese team's offense and defense, the defense is still incomplete, but it is still higher than the Chinese team. Therefore, the Chinese team will definitely be defeated. In short, the outcome of this Games depends entirely on the defensive strength of each team. This is often overlooked by people, but you must know that offense is the best defense. It is impossible to shoot if you always stand under the basket waiting for the ball. If you always think of the enemy coming to attack and pay attention to defense, you will have the opportunity to attack the enemy. It seems that none of the three teams paid much attention to this point.

The Chinese team cannot discuss the team's overall tactical plan or individual advances and retreats. In the eyes of outsiders, there are too many things that are inappropriate. I will not list them one by one. However, Mr. Tang Baokun's agile skills and Mr. Li Guochen's calm playing style are indeed rare talents. Individual skills in the Games should be the best of the two.

Criticism from the Games Referee, Mr. Higashijo

The Chinese team's offensive is exclusively using the straight attack method, and no one is active on both sides, which is the biggest weakness. Every time they attack, they send Mr. Tang straight into enemy territory without regard to the guards on both sides of the enemy. After the enemy's guards steal the ball, they retreat to the two sides and pass the ball to each other to advance. Although Mr. Tang runs back and forth, it is all in vain. Center Liu Jianchang and guard Li Guochen are fast and steady, and they are not flustered or hurried. They are truly outstanding in the army.

One of the most incomprehensible points in our tactics of the Chinese team is that in the second half of the second game between China and the Philippines, Mr. Tang Baokun and Mr. Chen Shengkui were on the court and their fighting power was very strong. They defeated the Soviet army with a score of 15 to 30 and could have taken advantage of the situation to continue scoring. However, coach Dong Shouyi suddenly replaced Chen Chengkui with Yao Enhan, and the Chinese team had no improvement. It can be said that the failure of the Chinese army this time was at the cost of this one substitution, which is not an excessive criticism.

The Chinese and Philippine teams were very embarrassed this time due to the Japanese refereeing. This is because the two teams lacked strict refereeing on weekdays. However, the Philippine army was still able to stabilize and fight back under unfavorable circumstances and win the final victory, while the Chinese team completely collapsed like a plate of loose sand. The individual spirit was confused and at a loss. This is nothing but a lack of experience. The only remedy is to play more games with stronger teams.

Words of Mr. Shiraro, the pioneer of the Japanese basketball community and sports director of the YMCA

The Chinese team has good performances in terms of individual skills, but it relies entirely on talent and lacks scientific training. Now basketball has become a science, and coaches must use scientific analysis methods. The most important first step is basic training, including (1) receiving or catching the ball, (2) passing the ball, (3) shooting, (4) step movements, and then gradually moving forward. This is undeniable. The Chinese team has the following obvious weaknesses:

(1) After the team members shoot, the team members themselves or teammates do not follow up, so the unmade shots are obtained by the enemy. (1) Although the center's rebounding is good, the rebounding position is too fixed, and because the forwards are short, the rebounded balls are repeatedly searched by the enemy. Under this circumstance, the center cannot change the direction of the rebound.

(1) When serving the ball from the boundary, the formation is too chaotic and there is no fixed offensive method, so the receiver often has no one to pass to and misses the opportunity.

(1) More effort must be put into firm receiving and accurate passing. The long-distance passing method should be used less.

(1) When the enemy uses the five-man defense method, the Chinese team specializes in concentrating the attack in the middle and does not know how to attack the weak points on both sides of the enemy area. This is a disadvantage of the accustomed vertical line attack method. In the future, at least more practice should be done with the horizontal line attack method.

Editor's note: The above three gentlemen are all first-class authorities in the Japanese basketball community. The articles are published in the most valuable magazines in Japan. The three gentlemen also have very detailed criticisms of the Japanese and Philippine teams. I will translate them again after Japan.

A Weekly Summary of the Gold Market

Market Trend... The Ending Was Extremely Charming

Increase... A Sum of Twenty-Three Taels

Difference... Thirty-Eight Taels and Change

A Bird's-Eye View of the Entire Week: The past week coincided with the end of the banks' semi-annual closing of accounts, with two days of holidays. Therefore, the gold exchange was also closed. Thus, only four days of market conditions were observed. The attitude towards the gold standard turned from weak to strong, but the waves were very turbulent, and people felt quite confused. Prices fluctuated by three or four taels to ten taels. As the silver market continued to decline and foreign exchange rates went from increasing to decreasing, the internal rate was looser than the listed rate, so arbitrage gradually became more appealing. At the beginning of the week, the price of gold once fell to 571 taels, as there were rumors that silver bullion had been shipped for export, and the large bars and drafts had increased in value, which had an impact. Towards the end of the week, it suddenly surged again, breaking through the 600-tael mark, as foreign merchants and British and American tobacco companies settled their accounts, and it was rumored that cash was being transported to Tianjin.

As a result, people's confidence greatly increased, and there was a rapid upward trend, reaching 609.3 taels. There was a difference of 38 taels and change in these few days, but the industry was confused and disoriented. The closing price was just over 607 taels, which was an increase of 23 taels compared to the end of the previous week. The initial bid price was more than 70 taels, and later it was 55 or 56 taels. The events that occurred during these four days, from June 30 (Monday) to July 5 (Saturday), are described in detail below.

Detailed Account of the Process: Since the beginning of the week (end of June), both British and American silver prices have increased, and foreign exchange rates have also increased. However, the internal market has turned tense, which can be described as seemingly loose but actually tight. The initial opening price for the August gold standard was 581 taels. Then, a large dealer sold off, and as the exchange rate had already increased by one and a half tiers, it suddenly fell to 571 taels. Then, buyers prevailed, and the rumor of government settlement resurfaced, so it turned upward again. In the afternoon, it reached 91 or 92 taels, so it actually increased by six or seven taels. However, the wind and waves were turbulent, and the market held a double settlement price. There were a total of 21 taels of twists and turns throughout the day. The next day, July 1 and 2, there was no market because of the bank holidays. By Thursday (the 3rd), the silver market had declined for three consecutive days, and the exchange rate had also decreased by two tiers. The internal market was also tight, causing the price of gold to break out of the 600-tael mark. Furthermore, large dealers such as Fuchang, Yuancheng, and Yongzheng competed to buy in the morning, with the gross price reaching 606 taels. In the afternoon, as the major dealers sold off, the 600-tael mark was broken. In the afternoon, it returned to its peak, but the total increase for the day was just over 11 taels. The final price increased by 10 taels and 7 mace. The market on the following day (Friday) seemed to be stable, with fluctuations of only five or six taels, and the price seemed to be reversing. Then, the large bars suddenly increased in value, and the exchange rate and other internal factors weakened. As a result, it returned to 597.3 taels, a sharp drop of 4 taels and 6 mace. By Saturday (the 5th), the British silver was unchanged, and the American silver was not traded. The exchange rate did not move, and the internal market became tight again. Thus, the price of gold once again broke out of the 600-tael mark. However, the various firms had different inflows and outflows, and the price level was still good. However, there were 11 taels of twists and turns in half a day, and the exchange rate and other factors suggested that settlements were being made and that cash was being shipped to Tianjin. The market atmosphere suddenly became sharp, but the drafts were only slightly firm, not as sharp as the price of gold, and arbitrage was approaching. The opening price in the morning was the lowest, at 98.2 taels. At noon, it jumped by 10 taels, reaching 609.3 taels. The closing price was 607.5 taels, an increase of 10 taels and 2 mace compared to the previous day. The spot price was especially high and should have been increased by seven or eight taels, as the outflow seemed to be active. Compared to June 28 (the previous Saturday), it had increased by 23 taels, which was a significant change. The difference between the highest and lowest prices this week was 38 taels and 3 mace. The following table lists the high and low peaks for British and American silver markets and drafts:

Type Highest Lowest Compared to Last Saturday
