Securities 88

Weekly Review of the Bond Market Before and After the Account Settlement

Bond Prices Continue to Fall Sharply, Transactions Approach 40 Million

Due to the timing of the semi-annual account settlement, the bond market in Shanghai experienced significant price fluctuations, but the market appeared calm as major players remained on the sidelines. Except for Tuesday and Wednesday, when the market was closed for account settlement, futures trading amounted to over 12.4 million on Monday and over 11.1 million on Saturday. On Thursday and Friday, it was approximately 8 million each, totaling 39.52 million. Among them, Customs bonds, Reorganization bonds, and Disbandment bonds were the most active. Customs bonds for July totaled 6,665,000 yuan, and for August, 4,070,000 yuan. Reorganization bonds for July totaled 7,915,000 yuan, and for August, 3,965,000 yuan. Disbandment bonds for July totaled 7,600,500 yuan, and for August, 2,080,000 yuan. Rehabilitation bonds were also good, with 2,745,000 yuan for July and 1,490,000 yuan for August. Other bonds were quiet, such as the Sixth Year bonds, with 920,000 yuan for July and 980,000 yuan for August; Continued bonds, with 815,000 yuan for July and 20,000 yuan for August; Continued Second Five bonds, with only 500,000 yuan for July; Seventh Year bonds, with 100,000 yuan for July and 30,000 yuan for August; and the Ninety-Sixth Year bonds, with 90,000 yuan for July and 10,000 yuan for August. Financial bonds only opened with 20,000 yuan for July. Spot trading amounted to only 57,600 yuan, with Reorganization bonds accounting for 25,100 yuan and others only a few thousand yuan. In addition, the Nineteenth Year Customs bonds and Cigarette bonds have been opened for spot trading, but the circulation in the market is limited, and there will not be a large volume of transactions for the time being. The trend of bond prices is becoming increasingly tense due to the political situation. The market is feeling uneasy, and sellers are dominating. Although the price has fallen sharply, there are still many people taking the opportunity to buy in the market, but the supply and demand situation is still very different. Regarding the changes, except for Thursday, when the market sentiment stabilized slightly and the price rebounded, with Customs bonds, Reorganization bonds, Rehabilitation bonds, and other futures each rising by about 1.5 yuan, the rest continued to fall step by step, with a very consistent trend. On the last day of the weekend, the decline was particularly severe. The Disbandment bond futures were almost suspended due to excessive declines. As a result, compared to the previous week, Reorganization bond spot prices fell by more than 6 yuan, and Disbandment bond futures continued to fall by about 4.56 yuan. Customs and Reorganization bond futures also fell by more than 23 yuan. Except for the Ninety-Sixth Year bonds, which remained stable, other bonds also generally continued to fall. The current situation in the bond market is such that unless the political situation improves temporarily, bond prices will not easily return to firmness in the short term. Silk and Tea 90

The Silk Market Last Week Was on the Brink of Collapse

New York Silk Market Plunges to New Low Since the Start of the Great War

English and French Prices Open with Small Differences, Factory Cost 200 Taels

Last week, the Shanghai foreign firm silk market was the first week after the account settlement period for various foreign firms. In previous years, there was usually new transaction development at this time. This year, drastic changes have occurred in the Chinese and foreign silk markets, making it almost impossible to salvage the situation. The reason is that Chinese silk has always relied on American sales as its center, and the United States is currently the largest consumer of raw silk in the world. However, since the announcement and implementation of the new tariff bill, the economy has suddenly changed. In addition, silk fabrics are sluggish and inventories are piled up, so silk mills have had to reduce work, stop machines, and switch to using rayon to maintain the current situation. Silk prices have plunged, with a drop of two, three, to seven, eight dimes in US dollars per pound. Silk mills in England and France are also focusing on rayon in order to maintain workers' jobs, and there are only sporadic transactions in raw silk, and the opening prices are surprisingly small, with a difference of 200 taels from the cost of Shanghai factories. Chinese silk merchants are all concerned that the spring and summer cocoons have been poor, and the cost of silk is not cheap, and the loss is too great, making it difficult to sell. The silk market was almost stagnant last week. The low prices of overseas silk have set a new record since the start of the European War. The prospects for the silk market are increasingly pessimistic. Last week was the first week after the British and French postal ship companies increased the freight rates for Chinese silk. There are only 300 pieces of raw silk shipped to the United States. The following table lists the prices of Chinese silk in overseas markets last week (New York: price per pound in US dollars; Lyon: price per kilo in French francs):

Laughing It Off 91

Hai Ke

Woman: The earrings you gave me are really nice, but the two diamonds embedded on them are a little too small.

Man: Dear, I looked closely at your lovely little ears and then matched them. If I had embedded too large diamonds, it wouldn't have looked good because the size wouldn't match.

A: When Mr. C was first in love with Miss D, his heart was really hot. He had to buy a large bouquet of roses and send them to her house every day.

B: What's it like now? Does he still send flowers to her?

A: Now he sends cauliflower.

B: Is it cauliflower to eat? How can you send that to your lover?

A: Because the two of them are married, and Mr. C always goes to the small vegetable market every morning.

Man: Oh my!

Woman: Madam, long time no see, I've forgotten your name.

Woman: When we saw each other day and night, you had my name on your lips. No wonder you want to forget, but I've already married.

Husband: When you see Mr. Wang next door, you must be more serious. If I see you acting frivolous like today, I won't allow it.

Wife: I know, you've seen it today and yesterday, so I'll definitely change it up tomorrow.

Advocating Barley Rice 92

Hu Shuofu

Since the rice price problem occurred, many parties have been trying to find a solution, and especially those who advocate eating wheat are the most numerous. It is also said that northerners like wheat and are strong, while southerners like rice and are weak. Wheat prices are cheap, and rice prices are expensive, so it should be possible to implement reforms immediately. Unfortunately, flour is also expensive, so the so-called eating wheat should be to grind barley and naked barley to remove their skin and cook them with a little rice to make rice, or even without any rice at all. This is what the ancients called barley rice. Now, not being familiar with it, I will briefly describe the barley rice recorded in ancient books as follows, so that everyone knows that advocating eating barley rice is not a new invention:

Wu Yue Chunqiu: Wu Yuan arrived at the Jiang River, and a fisherman in the river ferried him across the Qianxun Ferry, holding barley rice, abalone soup, and a jar of wine, and singing and calling, "A person in the reeds, a person in the reeds, isn't he a poor scholar?"

Ji Jiu Pian: Pancakes, wheat rice, sweet bean soup

Hou Hanshu, Biography of Feng Yi: Wang Lang raised up, and Guangwu rushed southeast from Ji to Nangong. He encountered a great wind and rain. Guangwu led the chariot into a vacant house by the side of the road. Yi offered wheat rice and rabbit shoulder.

Hou Hanshu, Biography of Jing Dan: Marquis Yinyang, Yin Jiu, robbed and brought Dan. Having no choice, he set up a meal of barley rice and scallions.

Qi Shu, Biography of Liu Huaiwei: A civilian offered a dou of new rice. Huaiwei brought out the barley rice he was eating and showed it to him, saying, "I have more than enough to eat in the morning, so I don't need to bother with this."

Bei Shi, Wei Xiaowu Emperor Ji: The emperor whipped his horse and galloped to Hucheng. He was very hungry and thirsty. A villager from Sansi Village offered barley rice and a jug of wine. The emperor enjoyed it and rewarded the village for ten years.

Su Shi's poem: The west of the city suddenly reports the arrival of an old friend, so I quickly sweep the wind porch and cook barley rice.

Fang Yue's poem: The aroma of barley rice from the east family is strong, the west family sells silk and trades new grain.

Briefly listing historical events and poems by poets, it can be seen that eating barley rice has been around for a long time. Today, to solve the problem of expensive rice, eating barley rice is the most appropriate. It is hoped that someone will advocate it.

Random Talk about Wuhu 93

Qian Qian

It has been ten days since I left Shanghai and arrived in Wuhu. I have carefully observed the customs and human sentiments of Wuhu, and I still don't see how closed-off it is. This is probably due to the convenience of transportation and the development of commerce. I have heard and seen a lot in these ten days, so I write it down randomly.

It can be said that Wuhu today is not impossible.

Silver Horns Are Not Current: Double mill silver coins are not very current here. Those who must exchange them at exchange shops must determine the price based on the silver coin. Generally, those from the eighth and eleventh years of the Republic of China are not current. Those from the ninth and tenth years can only be exchanged for 38 to 40 copper coins per coin. The silver coins I brought this time are still placed in a box, as I would rather leave them for use when I return to Shanghai. The current ones are all silver dollar bills and copper coins, with each silver dollar exchangeable for 320 copper coins.

Shops Have Two Prices: Most shops have a bargaining price. Those with marked prices, like Sincere and Wing On in Shanghai, are only four or five. Those who first arrive in Wuhu from Shanghai are greatly taken advantage of by the shops. The custom in shops is like this. Although it is clear that this is a weakness, the psychology of the buyer seems to require bargaining, so it is difficult to change it immediately.

It Is Difficult to Enjoy the Cool in Wuhu: Wuhu has a lake called Wuhu, but it is only a few miles around. There are also small boats in the middle that are enough to sail on. However, the lake is a dead water and does not connect to rivers. Recently, the water has turned green and has a strange odor. Small restaurants such as the First Spring, Yile Spring, and Second Western Restaurants on Zhongshan Road, as well as Yipin Xuan and Yipin Xiang Second Chinese Restaurants, all have water pavilions built, where people gather to drink in the evening, and the cool breeze is gentle. However, sometimes the wind and odor come together, and it is truly unbearable to approach.

Discussion of the National Goods Company: Recently, Mr. Hong Wenbin has newly joined forces to set up a National Goods Company to sell department store goods on a large scale, like the Sanyou Industrial Society in Shanghai. The roof item has a drink ice room, and the goods are sold at a fixed price and are all domestic goods, which shows patriotism and enthusiasm. The Wuhu Wanjiang Daily's attached column "Jungle Talk" has recently published many articles discussing the arrogance of the company's employees and the issue of the female employees' limelight, and Mr. Hong has also answered them one by one, which has attracted the attention of the general public. I think if there is indeed such a thing, it may be reformed. The newspaper industry should only fulfill its responsibility of guiding and correcting, and should not be too demanding. I think Mr. Hong will also agree with my opinion.

Sound Films Shown in Trains 95

Bi Ren

Sound films can be said to be popular today. However, I have never heard of them being shown in trains. It started with the Union Pacific train. When the train crossed the vast Colorado Desert, the small theater in the train showed sound films, allowing the dreary and boring passengers to enjoy the pleasure of viewing and listening.

This mobile cinema is attached to the Union Pacific train and is a trial run by Paramount Pictures, in conjunction with General Electric Production Research Company and Union Pacific Company.

The contents of the theater are all planned and configured by Paramount's professional technicians in Hollywood, and the decoration is very luxurious and beautiful. The seats are comfortable. All the machines that should be available for showing sound films are available. The first film to be shown is "The Virginian," starring Gary Cooper.

When the train with the cinema car arrives in New Mexico and Las Vegas, it separates from the original train and changes to another car to return to Los Angeles. Passengers can still enjoy the novel entertainment. I heard that the planning period lasted almost a year before such success was achieved.

南洋 Travelogue 96

(44) Spiritual Flower

On the 14th, I visited a Mr. Someone from the Overseas Chinese Middle School to discuss the New Villages in Nanyang. He had operated in the eastern provinces and failed due to the unrest. He had also seen my New Village Covenant. I told him that the New Village sites within the country were in the north in Suiyuan and Hetao. There were none in the south like Guangxi. Guangxi could establish a New Village for thousands of people. With thousands of people, land could be obtained from the government. It would be best to establish a New Village after the unrest subsided. He said his home was in Hunan, close to Guangxi. In the past, Liu Zihou's writings greatly praised the beauty of Hunan's mountains and rivers, saying they were rarely found anywhere else in the world. People who lived there would think they were immortals. I asked him about it, but he was a writer and likely embellished too much. However, Tao Yuanming's Record of the Peach Blossom Spring was also attributed to Wuling in Hunan and is still a mystery today. He said that New Villages in Nanyang could be found, and funds could be raised. The future looks promising.

On the 15th, I visited the botanical gardens. There were many plants in the garden that ordinary people could not name. Moreover, tropical plants are completely different from northern plants, and their properties are also different. The garden was established in 1874 and covers approximately 350 acres. The garden has a slightly elevated slope with a pond below, but Singapore has no mountains, only flat land everywhere, so there is not much difference in elevation. There is a Mango tree. This fruit is quite expensive in Shanghai, costing two dimes each. At first, its taste can be intoxicating. Tropical fruits often have a wine-like flavor, and I am not used to eating them. There is also a Durian tree. Durian is a very large and expensive fruit. It is covered with thorns. Each one costs four or five dimes or more here. It is not produced on this island but comes from the countryside. It is as big as a watermelon, so if one of these fruits fell from above in the garden, it could kill someone. The same is true for coconuts. Although they are not as big as durians, if one hit you on the head, it could break your skull. The durian is named Durian. When we first eat it, we can't stand its smell. But once you get used to it, you have to eat it, as if you were addicted. I then thought that everything in the world is a matter of habit. Perfume and stench are reversed. Only in food and drink is there no fixed taste. Zhuangzi said, "Deer eat reeds, people eat grain-fed meat, and dung beetles eat dung. Who knows the true taste?" This is like saltwater fish in the sea die in freshwater, and freshwater fish cannot survive in saltwater. There is an Asoka tree SorrowLesstree, which, like the Bodhi tree, is treasured in Buddhist countries. There are also Guanyin bamboo and bamboo forests. Although there are not many bamboo forests here, they are often seen. I saw very lush and beautiful bamboo forests in Guangxi. I heard that in Quanzhou, north of Guilin, there are hundreds of varieties in forests stretching for several miles. There is not much bamboo in Nanyang, but it would be good to plant more to create beautiful scenery. I wrote a poem on the aesthetics of bamboo in Guilin, which I am very proud of. The ancients compared bamboo to virtue. The clarity and beauty of bamboo is essential among plants. Nanyang, a hot place, should be planted with bamboo to dissipate the blazing heat.

Discussion of Electric Lights in Western Plays 97

Qi Rushan

Before fully describing the use of electric lights in Western plays, I must solemnly declare that I am a layman in optics, and I have no in-depth research on the use of light in drama. I am only reporting what I have seen to my fellow comrades. Zhang Pengchun and Yu Jiu, two gentlemen, said that Mr. Zhao Taimou has done extensive research on this topic, but unfortunately, I have not had the opportunity to learn from him. Twenty years ago, when I traveled in Europe, I paid close attention to the lighting methods used in theaters in various countries. However, at that time, the research in various countries was limited to describing the scenes of the sun and moon, day and night, water, fire, smoke, clouds, wind, rain, darkness and light, distance, strength, and weakness. There was no deep study of how light could move the audience. I have not been to Europe in the past ten years. I imagine there has been rapid progress. This year, when I came to the United States with Mr. Mei Lanfang, I saw that the lighting methods used in the theaters were different. Some used direct light, some used reflected light, some used dim light, and some used curved light. In some theaters, you could not see a single light, but there was still enough light. The audience was immersed in it as if sitting outdoors under the open sky. The color coordination could be described as ever-changing. When I entered the backstage organization, I saw that the research and equipment for lighting were given an important position. Many of the raw materials came from Germany, and there were also many machines invented in America. I heard that there was a newly invented machine that could change over ninety colors in one minute. The entire machine was worth over ten thousand US dollars. The research and evolution are truly advancing by leaps and bounds. One day, Mr. Bel Geddes, a master of optics and architecture, came to visit. He greatly admired Mr. Mei. We had a very pleasant conversation. I inquired about his lighting methods, so he invited me to see his work and enter his studio the next day. I saw it was full of optical architecture drawings. The equipment for the scenery and the effect of emotions were all changed by light. There were also two latest theater design blueprints, one for the architecture of the 1933 Chicago Art Exhibition and one built on the lake. There were seats and boxes, and the audience could row boats freely. The lighting equipment was different from that of ordinary theaters. One was built at the bottom of the lake. The entrance path was shallow and gradually deepened. The sides of the path were decorated with glass to prevent water from entering, and various colors of electric lights were arranged so that the audience felt like they were entering the bottom of the sea when they entered the theater. The various lights in the theater imitated the scenery of the seabed. The audience sat as if they were in a crystal palace. Although the use of light in theaters has reached its peak, it is still only used in the performance itself. Here, the lighting of the audience area is also being carefully researched. What I have discussed above is still using light as an aid to the performance. Recently, Mr. Wilford, a master of optics, invented a machine specifically to move people's psychology with light. One day, he invited Mei Lanfang, Zhang Pengchun, and me to see his machine. When I entered his room, I saw many machines and various designs were displayed everywhere. The newest machine had six light heads. The machine was like a square disk, five or six feet in length and width. Small mechanisms were arranged like a star chart on the disk surface, all with very precise scales. By pushing and pressing with both hands, the light projected from the lamps onto the screen changed endlessly. First, he tried with triangular light, then he tried with light similar to landscape, and the light had a meaning. In short, it was sometimes like still water at the bottom of a well, sometimes like boiling soup in a cauldron, sometimes like a pile of brocade, sometimes like a group of beauties playing in the waves, sometimes like drizzle, sometimes like a gentle breeze, sometimes like endless falling leaves, sometimes like the endless Yangtze River, sometimes like an old monk in meditation, sometimes like an angry lion roaring, sometimes white waves surging, sometimes auspicious clouds gathering, sometimes thunder and lightning, sometimes the wind stops and the clouds clear, sometimes like ten thousand miles of plains, sometimes like a thousand-foot cliff, sometimes like clouds and horses flying in the sky, sometimes like a group of swans playing in the sea, sometimes like deep mountains and great swamps, sometimes like a secluded spring in an empty valley, sometimes the earth shakes and the mountains sway, sometimes the wind is calm and the waves are still, sometimes like being in the clouds, sometimes like being hidden at the bottom of the sea, sometimes the mind is relaxed and happy, and sometimes it is thrilling. The light on the screen changed repeatedly, and the audience's mind also changed with it. It was truly a spectacle of optics. According to Mr. Wilford, the research is not yet precise, and the psychology of ordinary people has not yet been moved, so he dares not put it on the market. After further research, he will undoubtedly achieve his goal. The perseverance of Western scholars in scientific research is admirable. Outside the room, there were also several small machines that could be carried around, which could also change several kinds of light, but not as many changes as the large machine. When asked how much they cost, he replied that they were not yet complete, so they were not for sale at the moment. In the future, each machine would cost about two or three thousand gold. The research of light has reached a point where it is completely separate from the drama. The more various sciences are researched, the more specialization is needed. This is inevitable. Overall, the research on electric light can be described as leaving no stone unturned. The viewers also felt relaxed and happy. It is an important invention. Unfortunately, Chinese opera cannot use it at the moment. When Mr. Mei was in New York, there were two great directors, Mr. Earl Corrv. They also had extensive research on light. Before Mr. Mei performed, he said that drama must be equipped with electric light here. I will help especially. I have a good relationship with each theater, and if I suggest it, the theater will be happy to do so. He was very sincere and touching. He was immediately asked to take care of the arrangement of the theater. Mr. Kuo first went to each play site to carefully study the distribution of electric lights. The ten kinds of light changes pointed out by his fingers resulted in using white light from beginning to end without changing. Because Chinese dramas are symbolic. Whether day or night, darkness or light, are all expressed through movements and expressions. If supplemented by light, it will not only be useless but also harm the plot. Take various objects, such as door curtains, hall curtains, table skirts, chairs, costumes, decorations, etc., they are all in very dark colors. No matter what kind of electric light is projected onto them, it will lose its effect. Therefore, the current Western set designs are mostly lightly sketched, relying entirely on light to change the color. As for dance, acrobatics, etc., most of the scenes are monochrome curtains, and the costumes are only one or two kinds of very light colors. At that time, electric light is used to transform and change many colors, which is very beautiful. If you use heavy colors of dark red and green, electric light will be useless. This is also the current situation of the use of electric light in Western plays. Therefore, if Chinese dramas also adopt electric light in the future, there must be a completely different type of organization method to be able to control it.

City Government Allocates 1,000 Yuan for Locust Control 100

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau believes that locusts have been causing disasters and damaging crops recently. According to the investigation report of the Insect Bureau of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi provinces, the loss in Jiangsu Province in the 18th year of the Republic was 10 million yuan. The loss in Zhejiang Province was 10 million yuan in the 17th year and nearly 40 million yuan in the 18th year. The total loss in Jiangxi Province in the 17th and 18th years was 19 million yuan. Although this city has not conducted a detailed investigation, according to the report of the Zhenru Agricultural Experiment Field of the Chinese Agricultural Society, the yield per mu in the 17th year must be reduced by 25%. If the area occupied by rice in the urban area accounts for two-tenths of the total area, which is about 140,000 mu, and the average yield is reduced by 80 catties per mu, the loss due to locusts should be more than 700,000 yuan. The degree of locust damage in the 18th year was increased by 50% compared with the 17th year, and the estimated loss was more than 1 million yuan. The harm of locusts is evident. The bureau approved the city government's allocation of funds for locust control last year and compiled and printed various locust control illustrations and slogans, purchased specimen equipment and sent personnel to various districts to carry out propaganda, and selected the more severely affected districts to conduct a pilot locust control cooperation experiment area. The entire process of handling the matter has been reported to the city government for filing. It is now approved by the Baoshan County Government to forward the letter from the Secretariat of the Agricultural College of the National Labor University, stating that locust eggs were found in the four agricultural areas. They are transferring the search and capture of locust moths and burning locust eggs in order to prevent rice disasters and save farmers. The bureau sent personnel to various districts with various propaganda materials to conduct extensive persuasion. At the same time, the Labor University Agricultural College was requested to assign experts to assist. According to the report of the returning personnel, when they went to various districts to conduct propaganda, very few farmers came to listen to the lectures. If the goal of eliminating locust damage and enriching people's welfare is to be achieved, it is feared that there will be no hope if another way is not sought. The bureau reported to the city government for review. The extermination of locusts is the only good way to save people's food. If farmers are not urged to work hard to eliminate the hidden dangers, it is unbearable to imagine. In order to fundamentally save agriculture the bureau intends to purchase locust moths and locust eggs in various districts of the city in order to extinguish and save the people. It specially requests the city government to approve the allocation of 1,000 yuan for locust control in accordance with the case. It is proposed to cooperate with the Labor University Academy to purchase extensively in Wusong Jiangwan and other districts first. The temporarily determined purchase price is one copper coin for each locust egg block and two copper coins for each two locust moths. It is heard that the city government, after receiving the report, specifically ordered the approval of the matter relating to the prevention of rice disasters and at the same time, ordered the Finance Bureau to allocate 1,000 yuan for expenses.

Shanghai County Locust Control Campaign Yesterday's News 101

The Shanghai County locust control publicity campaign was decided by the county government in a meeting the day before yesterday to be carried out in districts. Yesterday morning, the county government sent personnel accompanied by locust control expert Chen Mengshi to the fourth district of Pudong and Sanlintang to meet with Chief Bi of the district to hold a publicity meeting. Qu Liangshi Invites Celebrities to Exhibit His Book Collection 102

The book collection of the Qu family's Tieqin Bronze Sword Building in Changshu is known as one of the four major book collectors along with the Yang family's Haiyuan Pavilion, the Lu family's Song Tower, and the Ding family's Rare Book Room. Later, the Lu books went to the Iwasaki Library in Japan, and the Ding books went to the Nanjing Library. Although the Yang books were recently banned from being transported out by the Shandong Provincial Government, they have been inevitably scattered. Only Qu Diyiye's collection has not been scattered. The entire collection has been stored in Yu County. After the Qi Lu War in the year of Ji Chou, fearing that they would suffer from war again, he specifically moved them to a refined residence in Shanghai. Yesterday, the owner, Qu Liangshi, specially invited literary figures Cai Yuanpei, Hu Shi, Dong Zuobin, Zhang Yuanji, and others to visit. All the Song and Yuan editions listed in the original catalog were present, and they were all surprised by the far-reaching nature of the collection. Rumors in the outside world saying that he was trying to sell them to foreign countries for profit are completely unfounded.

The Second Day of the Joint Movement Propaganda Week 103

Academic Lectures in the Morning, Recreational Activities in the Afternoon

Recreational Gathering Will Continue at the Youth League Tonight

Yesterday was the second day of the Cooperative Movement Propaganda Week in the city. The organizing committee sent letters to various sectors beforehand to notify them that an academic lecture on cooperation would be held at Daxia University on Jiaozhou Road, Shanghai, at 9:00 am, and a recreational gathering would be held at the City Chamber of Commerce on Tianhou Palace Bridge in the afternoon. The details are recorded below.

More than 200 people attended the meeting. First, Chairman Xu Xingchu gave a report, stating briefly that today is the second day of the Cooperative Movement Propaganda Week in the city. Holding an academic lecture here makes the urgency of the cooperative movement needed in our country is known to all. However, in order to promote the cooperative business effectively, we must first know and then act, otherwise, it will fail. Since the beginning of the cooperative movement in various countries around the world, there have been many cases of failure due to this mistake. The organizing committee, in view of Ster, invited cooperation experts to give lectures so that the city's cooperative business can be promoted without hindrance. The central government has issued an order to all provinces and cities across the country to hold a cooperative movement propaganda week. The significance of this is to save China's dying people's livelihood. The city's cooperative movement propaganda week is jointly prepared by party and government agencies. Holding a recreational gathering here today is to promote the theory and methods of organizing cooperative societies in the minds of the general public in order to achieve great progress in the city's cooperative business after the end of the party's propaganda week. He hopes that all those present will understand this meaning, then the city's cooperative business will surely succeed before other places. Then, the performance of recreational programs began. There were many programs and they cannot all be listed. There were many propaganda materials in the venue, and everyone who attended got a copy, reading with great interest the various issues of the cooperative society. It was not until about 12 o'clock that the meeting was adjourned.

Recreational gathering Tonight at 7:00 pm tonight, the organizing committee will hold a cooperative movement propaganda recreational gathering at the Youth Propaganda Team in Xiaoximen, Nanshi, by the first and second district party headquarters. Experts and celebrities are invited to give lectures, and various groups will perform national arts, new dramas, songs, dances, and dialogues to add to the fun. Yu Tang Funding 107

Requesting Additional Tax on Fields

Yang Fulin, Chairman of the Yu Tang Dredging Preparatory Committee, presented a document to the Shanghai County Government and the Construction Bureau yesterday, stating that it was a report on the decision to dredge the Yu Tang and carry out additional tax on the fields, requesting review and forwarding. The dredging of the Yu Tang was organized on September 10 of the 18th year by the district chiefs of the second, third, and sixth districts and the director of the Construction Bureau to organize a preparatory committee to discuss the dredging methods. The charter of the preparatory committee and the list of members have been reported for filing. However, the river is the main river in the east and west of the county, receiving the Xiepu River in the east and reaching the Yueerjing in the Songjiang boundary to reach the Mao River, which is more than 4,700 feet long. In particular, the East Huangpu River receives the incoming tide and turbid outflow, and sediment is easily deposited, which is becoming increasingly blocked. The dredging project this time is huge, and the funding is even greater. Therefore, the fourth and fifth preparatory committee meetings decided to implement the project, referring to the Xiecheng case of the dredging of the Yu Tang in the Tongzhi period, reducing the amount of Xie dredging by half, issuing the river rice to the owners, and halving the Xie dredging according to the large dredging example of five liters per mu. The dredging funds, excluding the survey fee borne by the Construction Bureau, are fixed at 10,000 yuan, estimated as follows: (1) Bridge repair fee of 3,000 yuan (2) Fill fee of 2,500 yuan (3) Water fee of 2,000 yuan (4) Level pile fee of 500 yuan (5) Office fee of 1,000 yuan (6) Reserve fee of 1,000 yuan is generally collected from the fields and taxes. The association separately submits it to the county bureau and forwards it to the financial and construction departments for review, etc. With the approval of this, it should be copied and submitted to the above-mentioned resolution for review and approval to forward and approve the additional tax on the fields in order to seek water conservancy and benefit the people, which is convenient for the public.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Explains the Labor Dispute Resolution Law 108

The Shanghai Commercial Press trade unions requested a general wage increase, resulting in a labor dispute. The Shanghai Municipal Government's arbitration was ineffective and difficult to handle. The Shanghai Municipal Government's detailed rules for the implementation of the Labor Dispute Resolution Law and the separate regulations and interpretations on the meaning and scope of employment conditions of worker groups, as well as how to remedy the special circumstances where arbitration committee members refuse to attend and cannot arbitrate, have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for review and approval, which was consulted by the Judicial Yuan and ordered the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to reply. It is learned that the department has submitted the meaning interpretation for review, stating briefly that the issue of whether the absence of members of the Labor Arbitration Committee can open the arbitration has been presented by the Shanghai Municipal Government to the Executive Yuan, instructing the Judicial Yuan to interpret that if the members of the arbitration committee are unable to perform their duties, a separate meeting should be held depending on which item of Article 13 the member represents. The same shall be followed and replaced. However, if the special circumstances mentioned in the original application are not remedied, not only will the parties to the dispute suffer, but the original intention of the legislation will be lost. It is believed that since the representatives of the fourth item of Article 13 of the Labor Dispute Resolution Law have been recommended by the worker groups and employer groups, they must have considerable qualifications in the worker groups or employer groups, and the task of the arbitration committee is to be fair and seek the interests of both labor and management, which is the responsibility that should be fulfilled after being recommended and approved. Therefore, if an arbitration committee member cannot perform their duties due to some reason before the meeting, they should state the reasons and be permitted by the original convening agency to appoint a representative with the same qualifications to fill the vacancy. If they do not declare an obstacle and do not attend, it will be deemed that the representative has voluntarily given up, and the original convening agency will report it to the government to remove their qualifications as an arbitration committee member from the list of arbitration committee members and report it to the department for filing as a reputational punishment so that they can be warned and maintain the law. Although there is no clear provision in the labor dispute law for this method, it can be clearly stipulated in the implementation rules prepared by each province and city to remedy it.

Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Representatives Go to Beijing to Petition 109

Restore the Boundaries of Traditional Business Sectors

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Dyeing Trade Association, the Shanghai Silk and Satin Dyeing Workers' Union, and the Shanghai Cotton and Cloth Dyeing Workers' Union, representing both labor and management, have been jointly discussing the disruption of their business by outsiders and the resulting threat to labor and management. They have resolved to send representatives, including Zhu Boying, to Beijing with a petition last night by train to appeal to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government's Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. They request the implementation of relief measures. The petition reads as follows:

A Petition for the Implementation of Relief Measures to Address Business Disruption and Harm to Labor and Management, in order to Maintain Industry and Commerce and Benefit the People.

It is respectfully stated that Shanghai is the center of industry and commerce, and our dyeing industry is one of the material cultures related to silk and cotton weaving. It has a considerable history in the industrial sector, and its prosperity or decline is crucial to the national industrial economy and the people's livelihood. In recent years, with the eastward spread of Westernization, various imperialist powers have been using every means to carry out economic aggression, which has had a particularly significant impact on our dyeing industry. Furthermore, due to the lack of unity among businesses and the abandonment of industry regulations, dyeing prices have been excessively reduced, and the cost of dyes has suddenly increased, eroding capital. The inherent business is on the verge of decline, factories are closing one after another, unemployment among workers is increasing daily, and social security is precarious.

In view of this, the associations, in the spirit of labor-management cooperation, jointly organized the "Shanghai Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Labor-Management Joint Price Regulation Committee" in the winter. At the cost of material and spiritual sacrifices, they actively reorganized, unified dyeing prices, restored industry regulations, and properly arranged for unemployed workers. Past achievements have been fairly good, and the pitfalls of disputes in the second-hand clothing and pharmaceutical industries in Shanghai can be avoided. The recovery of business is just around the corner. However, recently, a group of red dye shops specializing in dyeing red, foreign yuan dye shops specializing in dyeing black, pre-refining shops specializing in primary refining, paddle shaft shops specializing in paddle shafts, and silk and satin stores that were not originally in the dyeing industry have taken the opportunity to carry out aggression, disrupting boundaries. They have openly accepted the dyeing of silk fabrics that were originally dyed by our silk and satin dyeing industry, reducing dyeing prices, cutting alcohol costs, and engaging in various disruptive and chaotic behaviors. If no measures are taken to stop and correct this, silk and satin dyeing factories will inevitably go bankrupt, and thousands of workers will become unemployed. What will become of our industry's future?

Although there are no explicit legal provisions regarding the scope of business in our commercial sector, established customs should not be abolished. Moreover, the Civil Code states, "Where there is no provision in the law, customs may be followed." The associations have repeatedly considered and negotiated, but to no avail. Although we have recently appealed to the local authorities in this city for relief, we fear that it may not be resolved in a timely manner. In order to protect the business and to liberate thousands of unemployed workers, in addition to separately submitting petitions to various agencies in this city for immediate and effective relief, we have dispatched representatives, including Zhu Boying, to present a written petition. We humbly request that you grant us an audience and promptly conduct comprehensive planning to implement relief measures. We also request that you instruct the responsible authorities in Shanghai to strictly prohibit and effectively correct the situation, restoring the boundaries of traditional business sectors in the shortest possible time, in order to protect industry and commerce and benefit the people. We await your instructions with utmost urgency.

Labor Dispute at French-Owned Water and Electricity Company 110

Hope for a Satisfactory Resolution

All Workers Scheduled to Resume Work This Morning

The labor dispute at the French-owned water and electricity company experienced unexpected complications regarding the resumption of work, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that there is hope for a satisfactory resolution, and all workers are scheduled to resume work this morning (the 7th) at 8:00 AM. The details are as follows:

Mediators Shuttle Back and Forth: After the news of the resumption of work encountered obstacles, the mediators, considering the complexity of the situation, were initially reluctant to intervene further. However, due to persistent requests from all parties, they dispatched representatives to shuttle back and forth, ultimately securing hope for a satisfactory resolution and a resumption of work at 8:00 AM today.

All Detained Workers Released: In addition to Zhou A'liu and Liu Linsheng, who have already been released, Song Youxing remains detained because he was transferred to the court by the Public Security Bureau and could not be released immediately. It is now learned that the mediators have taken responsibility for Song's release, and he is expected to regain his freedom today. Zhou A'long and two other workers, who were detained by the French police on the afternoon of the previous day, were also bailed out by the mediators at 3:00 PM yesterday and sent to the labor union.

Resumption of Work Plan Approved: At 3:00 PM yesterday, the workers convened a meeting of representatives to discuss the resumption of work plan, which included the following points: (1) The factory's agreement to the three conditions should be signed and implemented by the mediators in conjunction with the city party headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau. (2) Song Youxing should be released by tonight (the 7th). (3) The factory should completely remove the new workers and White Russians. (4) If disruptive elements continue to act as they did the day before, the French police should detain them. (5) The factory should open the gates when the workers resume work. It is reported that if the above plan cannot be achieved, the union will continue the strike. It is also reported that the strike committee and picket team organized by the union will not be disbanded for the time being and will only be dissolved after all the conditions have been met and work has officially resumed.

Two Orders from the County Reorganization Committee 113

District Party Departments and District Offices Need Not Hold Party-Government Talks

Executive and Supervisory Committee Members and Party Reorganization Committee Members May Not Serve Concurrently as District Chiefs

The Shanghai County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee, in accordance with the Provincial Reorganization Committee's order, stipulated that District Party Departments and District Offices need not hold Party-Government talks, and that Executive and Supervisory Committee Members and Party Affairs Reorganization Committee Members may not serve concurrently as District Chiefs. The committee issued orders to the districts yesterday, instructing them to comply accordingly. The two original orders are as follows:

(1) Order Regarding Compliance: In response to the Provincial Reorganization Committee's Order No. 215, it is stated: "Order for Implementation: An investigation reveals that the number of District Party Departments and District Offices in each county varies considerably. Often, a county has more than a dozen district branches, while the District Party Department has only two or three. Moreover, the designated locations also differ, and the location of the District Party Department may not necessarily be the location of the District Office. Although there was a proposal for District Party-Government talks, it is difficult to implement in practice. The 47th Committee Meeting of this Committee resolved that District Party Departments and District Offices need not hold Party-Government talks. In addition to sending instructions, it is imperative to record the order for your information and instruct your affiliated District Party Departments to be informed accordingly." In addition to issuing orders, it is ordered that the association strictly comply. This order.

(1) Notice Regarding Implementation: In response to the Provincial Reorganization Committee's Notice No. 214, it is stated: "Order for Compliance: The 47th Committee Meeting of this Committee resolved that Executive and Supervisory Committee Members and Party Affairs Reorganization Committee Members in each county may not serve concurrently as District Chiefs. In addition to sending instructions, it is imperative to record the order for your information and instruct everyone to comply strictly in order to emphasize work and avoid abuses. This order." In addition to issuing orders, it is ordered that the association be informed. This order.

Minutes of the Preparatory Meeting for the National Goods Emporium 117

The Preparatory Committee for the China National Products United Emporium held a meeting yesterday. Chairman Zhang Zilian first reported on the progress of the preparations, stating that the display and consignment departments had been organized. Mr. Wang Hanqiang has been appointed as the director of the display department, and Mr. Zhang Zixiang has been appointed as the director of the consignment department, effective immediately. The following matters were then discussed:

(1) Determining the number of staff for each department: It was resolved that each department should determine the number based on the actual situation.

(2) Revising the display method: It was resolved that those who have already participated in the emporium's business or consignment activities may submit samples for display without additional charges. Special products from other locations in China and abroad that do not occupy much space may also be displayed free of charge to promote them.

(3) Changing the status of the display and consignment departments: It was decided that the original consignment department would be renamed the display department, and the consignment department would be attached to the emporium.

(4) Determining the opening date: It was resolved that the emporium would open after all manufacturers have completed their arrangements. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Freight Trains on the Beijing-Shanghai Line 121

Collided Near Longtan Yesterday

Yesterday morning around 6:00 AM, after southbound freight train No. 44 on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway arrived at Longtan Station, locomotive B9 entered the Longtan China Cement Factory to haul approximately twenty loaded cars and parked on the station's branch line. It then entered the main line and parked at the east end of the station, intending to add water. At the same time, locomotive No. 69 of freight express train No. 372 also entered the main line, resulting in a collision. Fortunately, no major disaster occurred, but two axles on locomotive No. 69 of train No. 372 were damaged. It was not until 10:05 AM that rescue trains from both Beijing and Zhenjiang managed to repair the damage.

Reasons for Delays of Shanghai-Hangzhou Freight Trains on the Previous Two Days 122

Yesterday morning at 10:20 AM, freight train No. 21 from Zhapu to Shanghai on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway was approaching the junction west of Jiashan Station when the pointsman, due to illness and oversight, forgot to switch the points, causing the locomotive to derail the switch. Fortunately, the cars did not derail. The stationmaster telegraphed the engineering department to dispatch track workers and mechanics to repair the damage. The freight train was backed up to the original track to await repairs. After about five hours, the repairs were completed and traffic was restored, causing the freight train to arrive at the Shanghai station behind schedule.

On the night before last, freight train No. 27 from Zhapu to Shanghai was held up at Xieshi around 8:50 PM because workers from the road engineering department were repairing a bridge. The train was detained at the station until 4:40 PM the next day, arriving at the Shanghai station ten hours behind schedule.

Southern District of Shanghai 123

Defense Corps to Conclude Operations Immediately

Awaiting Reorganization

The team leaders of the Southern District of Shanghai Defense Corps received Instruction No. 124 from the Corps headquarters, "Order to Cease Operations and Await Reorganization, and Report the Completed Situation Within a Deadline." Team Leader Feng Runsheng of Team 3 considered the matter to be of great importance and notified all executive committee members, who convened an emergency meeting yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. It was resolved to comply with the order, cease operations immediately, await reorganization, and all committee members expressed their intention to resign. The original order is attached below:

Regarding Compliance: Instruction No. 90 from the Shanghai South District Office states, "In response to Instruction No. 250 from the Reorganization Committee, it is stated: 'Regarding the Instruction, it is paramount for all organizations to prioritize organization. The nature of the Defense Corps is similar to that of the military police, and its organization is particularly important. In the past, the Corps in various districts were established at different times and operated independently. There were no unified methods for funding and organization, and the content was disorganized and unclear. The number of people in the same team varied greatly, and the teams in the same Corps differed significantly. There were no standards for the number of teams to be established in each Corps or the number of people in each team, which had a significant impact on Corps affairs. Since this Committee was ordered to reorganize, the various points that needed to be rectified have been carried out in order, and the funding for the Corps in various districts has also been comprehensively planned and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval. In response to the organization level, repeated inquiries and deliberations have been made, and it has been decided that 108 people should be organized into one team, with each team having three squads and each squad having three shifts. The number of teams to be established in each district Corps should be based on the current number of Corps members and determined separately in consideration of local conditions, as resolved at the eleventh standing meeting. After this determination, the Corps in each district should immediately comply with the reorganization, and the number of personnel in each team must meet the prescribed quota and may not be deficient or excessive. Those who are currently insufficient should immediately recruit enough personnel, and those who have surplus personnel should be reassigned to the reserves. The allocation and combination of the Corps in each district and the distribution of defensive positions should still be considered and handled by the Corps chiefs based on local conditions. In addition to sending instructions, it is ordered that the chief immediately instruct the affiliated Corps in each district to comply uniformly and report the compliance situation within ten days from the date of this document so that personnel can be dispatched to verify the situation without any delay. This is extremely important.' In addition to issuing copies to various places, it is ordered that you immediately comply with the instructions and complete the handling of each item within ten days from the date of this document and report the compliance situation so that it can be forwarded for review without any delay. This is extremely important.' In response to this, it is ordered that each team should immediately cease operations and await reorganization, and that the team leader should immediately handle the conclusion and report it within three days from the date of this document to await transfer. This is extremely important."

Cloth Factory Merged into Mercerized Cotton Weaving Association 126

The Shanghai Mercerized Cotton Weaving Trade Association was officially established on April 26th of this year and has been approved by the Municipal Civil Training Committee and registered with the Social Affairs Bureau. Subsequently, representatives from the cloth factory industry, including Shen Yaoqing and fifty others, jointly submitted a petition to the Municipal Civil Training Committee requesting permission to establish a trade association. After receiving the petition, the Civil Training Committee dispatched personnel to inspect and review the matter. They determined that the business operated by the petitioners is similar to the business of the Mercerized Cotton Weaving Trade Association and should join the association in accordance with Article 5 of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law, which stipulates that only one trade association may be established for the same industry in the same area. It is learned that the petitioners have been instructed to comply and that the Mercerized Cotton Weaving Trade Association has been instructed to accept their membership and work together for the benefit of the industry.

Public Utilities Bureau Revises Procedures for Renewing Licenses for Plumbing and Electrical Supply Stores 127

Plumbing contractors, electrical supply stores, and electrical installers in the city are registering with the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, which issues licenses allowing them to operate. According to the Regulations for Registering Plumbing Contractors, plumbing contractor licenses are valid for one year and must be renewed upon expiration, with a renewal fee of two yuan. Those who continue to operate in the city with an expired license for more than fifteen days will be penalized if discovered. The Regulations for Managing Electrical Supply Stores and Electrical Installers also stipulate that electrical supply store or electrical installer licenses must be renewed annually. The bureau, recognizing that licensees often do not remember the expiration date and that there are too many to notify individually, has submitted a request to the Municipal Government to change the system so that plumbing contractor, electrical supply store, and electrical installer licenses must be renewed annually from July 1st to July 15th. Those whose licenses have been valid for less than six months will have their licenses renewed free of charge, while those whose licenses have been valid for more than six months but less than one year will pay half the fee. The new system will be implemented starting today.

Strange Egg in Baoshan 128

An Egg with a Small Hole

A Black Tail in the Hole

Can Move at Any Time

The Lei Ting Teahouse inside the West Gate of Baoshan is opened by the wife of the Mai family, Wang Lu. Mrs. Wang raises three hens. At 6:00 PM on the 5th of this month, the smallest hen laid a strange egg that was no different from ordinary eggs, except that the upper end of the egg had a dark shadow the size of a cash coin with a hole in the middle. A black tail, about an inch long and shaped like a rat's tail, protruded from the hole and could move on its own. This caused a sensation in the neighborhood, and onlookers flocked to see it. The incident was reported to the County Public Security Bureau, which ordered the patrol leader to borrow the egg from Mrs. Wang and place it in the City God Temple (i.e., the People's Assembly Hall) for the public to view. What is inside the egg will be reported after the eggshell is broken.

More Dangerous Than Floods and Wild Beasts 129

The Morphine Needle Machine

Needle Injectors Themselves Do Not Have This Addiction

Needle Addicts Have Injection Marks Like Honeycombs

Shao Changsheng Sentenced to Two Years Imprisonment

Seventeen People Sentenced to Six Months Imprisonment Each

Shanghai is an area where red and black poisons gather. The red one is the smoke cessation pill on the gun, commonly known as the "red bead," which is more than ten times more poisonous than black opium. It was not initially noticed by the world, and a large number of people from the mainland came to sell it. This is because the wholesale price in Shanghai is only seven or eight yuan per thousand, while it can be sold for eighteen or nineteen yuan or even more than twenty yuan in the mainland. Because of the profit, everyone is vying for it. Recently, military and police agencies have begun to strictly investigate and ban it at railway and wharf terminals, and there have been seizures from time to time. However, many Shanghai people with opium habits have changed to red pills because they are slightly cheaper than opium and the procedure is simple. However, ordinary coolies find that injecting morphine is even faster than red pills. According to insiders, a morphine injection worth one corner is enough to抵抵抵抵the effect of smoking opium worth three corners. Therefore, these people have abandoned opium and even red pills and only pursue injections. As a result, some people cater to the psychology of these people and set up a place for injections, specializing in passing golden needles to people all day long. The day before yesterday morning, Huishan Patrol Room Chinese detective Shi Baoying arrested seventeen coolies who were seeking morphine injections in a house at No. 29 Hua Ji Road. Observing their limbs, red and black spots were all over their skin, and there were many injection marks, shaped like honeycombs. From this, it can be seen that these seventeen people have been injecting not just for a day or two. Shao Changsheng, a native of Jiangbei who administered the injections, alone did not have this addiction. Considering the principle of "do not do to others what you do not want done to yourself," Shao is indeed guilty and cannot escape punishment. Subsequently, the patrol room sent them all to the Special District Local Court. Judge Ge Zhiqin interrogated them. Judge Ge sighed when he saw that they were emaciated and covered with scars. He warned them to quit as soon as possible, otherwise their death was not far off. Later, Shao Changsheng was sentenced to two years of imprisonment and fined four hundred yuan for engaging in this illegal act, and the other seventeen were each sentenced to six months of imprisonment, so that doctors could help them quit in prison. The morphine and injection equipment involved in the case were all confiscated.

A Dead Man in Bed 130

Avoiding Mosquitoes Leads to Disaster

Yang Yongyu Dies Strangely

Yang Yongyu, a 48-year-old machine worker from Zhenjiang, lived at No. 8, Tongkang Lane, Gaochang Temple, South Shanghai. Because the weather has been hot recently, and Gaochang Temple is a low-lying and humid area, mosquitoes buzzed and it was difficult to sleep at night. Yang and his wife, Yang Ma, were troubled by this. Therefore, after dinner the day before yesterday, Yang Ma discussed with her husband that it would be better to sleep elsewhere to avoid mosquitoes. So Yang Ma first went to her sister's house at No. 5 Zaopi Lane, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, to stay overnight, and made an appointment for Yang to go as well. Because Yang had other matters, he told his wife to go first and he would come later. After Yang Ma arrived at her sister's house, she asked to stay for a few nights, and her sister agreed. However, Yang Ma waited for her husband for a long time and had nothing to do to pass the long night. Her sister had two gambling tickets for the amusement park, so she went to play with her. When she returned home at midnight, Yang Yongyu was already lying on the bed, unconscious. When she pushed him, his body was stiff and his breath had stopped early on. She was greatly shocked and cried loudly. The police arrived and asked about the cause, and took Yang Ma to the 5th District Police Station. There were no clues, but the death of the deceased was strange and there were suspicious circumstances. Therefore, yesterday, Ge Yitu, the local保甲, was ordered to report to the local court for examination.

Forensic Preparation Office 131

To Build Autopsy and Tai Hospital

Since the Judicial Administration Department established the Forensic Preparation Office in the Special District Local Court, its most important work has been to prepare for the construction of an examination institute and the establishment of a hospital. In the past, autopsy examinations in the Public Concession were all conducted at the Autopsy Examination Institute on Fielun Road, and the examination was undertaken by the 工部局 Hospital next to the institute. Both places were under the jurisdiction of the 工部局. Now that our country has recovered the legal rights of the concession, the important task of examination should no longer be entrusted to foreigners. Therefore, the Forensic Preparation Office decided to build its own autopsy examination institute and hospital. It is said that the location has been surveyed along the Zhenru Town Railway and 民地 has been requisitioned. The drawings of the autopsy examination institute and hospital have been submitted to the Ministry of Justice for approval, and construction will begin immediately. The preparation office is now inviting contractors to bid, requiring completion within six months from the date of winning the bid.

Old Lu Gao Jian Meat Shop 137

Forced to Relocate and File a Lawsuit

The Old Lu Gao Jian Meat Shop at No. 312-4, Pintang Lane, Nanjing Road, has been open for more than ten years. The landlord is Zhang Hengshan, who has always been leased by the Gao Yi Mansion. On the 26th of last month, he suddenly received a notice from the agent,限 him to move out of the house the next day. The shop thought that the owner's forced relocation for no reason was wrong, and that the time limit was only one day, which was even more absurd. Moreover, the custom in Shanghai is that the landlord must give the tenant a month's notice of eviction. Now the landlord is forcing people too much, which is difficult to accept. He immediately hired lawyer E Sen to request the Special District Local Court to issue an edict prohibiting the landlord from forcing the relocation. However, the prohibition edict had not been issued by the 27th, and the landlord then ordered masons to remove the tiles from the shop, making it impossible to operate in the open air. The shop had to move. At the same time, it asked lawyer E to file a lawsuit against Zhang Hengshan for damages. It is said that the case will soon be summoned by the Special District Court for both parties to appear in court for trial.

According to news from the Shanghai Chinese Leprosy Relief Association, its Nanchang branch also plans to establish a leprosy hospital. However, due to frequent impact from the current situation and harassment by the Communist Party, it has been delayed. In view of the actual needs, it is difficult to delay any longer. At present, in addition to the subsidy from the provincial government of more than 1,800 yuan for the old leprosy hospital, which can be transferred, there is no funding for all the insufficient funds. The head office in Shanghai and the branch are now trying their best to raise funds separately to achieve the goal.

Responsibility Issues for Speculative Business

Manager Fang Shunyuan Accused

Liu Yusheng and others jointly hired a lawyer to file a criminal complaint in the French Concession Court, stating that the plaintiffs and defendant Fang Shunyuan jointly opened the Yiji Seafood Store in the administration a few years ago and elected the defendant as the manager. Unexpectedly, it closed down in March this year, after being open for one year and four months, with a total capital of 48,000 양. Now the loss is 70,000 양. Rumors are rife, saying that Yiji has suffered huge losses, so the shareholders had no choice but to declare liquidation. In this situation, the defendant clearly violated the crime of breach of trust and requested a trial, and should also bear civil liability. The defendant also pleaded through a lawyer that the plaintiff's accusation was unfounded. It should be known whether the 日金 transaction was proposed by the defendant personally or agreed by the shareholders. The Yiji seal was fully stamped on the transaction order. The seal has always been managed by the plaintiff Liu Qingcong, indicating that the 日金 transaction was actually made with the consent of the shareholders. Moreover, the red list at the end of the year clearly stated the speculative losses and was registered in the account book by the plaintiff, which can prove that this transaction was actually agreed by the shareholders. How can the defendant be held responsible?

The request is for a detailed investigation to dismiss the case. Judge Zhu instructed the defendant to pay a deposit and wait outside. Accountant Wu will investigate the accounts to determine whether the defendant should be held responsible and report back for verification.

Demanding Payment Leads to Conflict with a Blow to the Head 147

After paying off a certain amount at the end of the year, he still owes 7.6 洋. Yesterday, the shop sent shop assistants Chen Yongchang (22 years old) from Tongzhou and apprentice Cui Xiguang (17 years old) to demand payment. Qiao agreed to pay it off by the end of July. Unexpectedly, Chen and Cui were young and short-tempered, and a disagreement led to a conflict. Cui took the iron fork stick beside him and hit Qiao's head hard, causing a head injury and bleeding profusely. Qiao's wife called the police and brought Chen and Cui to the 1st Sub-Precinct of the 4th District for interrogation.

Hooligans砍 him with a Sharp Ax

The manager of the candied fruit department of the New Allen Cinema in Hongkou is Yu Guikun, a 25-year-old from Hunan. He has lost more than 100양 since he started his business in March. Usually, there are some hooligans who are used to eating for free. After eating, they disperse and generally do not pay. For the sake of his capital, Yu had to strictly refuse, which made them resent him. At around 11 am yesterday, three unfamiliar hooligans came to Yu and nodded to him as a courtesy. Afterwards, Patrol Post No. 1917 was called to accompany him to the Tongren Hospital for treatment by car.

Xiao Gouzi's Evil Nature is Inherent 152

He Stole from Neighbors at the Age of Ten

He Recently Stole Gold Rings and Silver Hairpins

Wen Qiyu, a boy from Tianjin, also known as Xiao Gouzi, is 14 years old and lives at No. 38 Luxi Street, Dongjiadu, Nanshi. The boy has always been bad-natured. He learned to be down-and-out at the age of ten and specialized in privately taking miscellaneous items and money from neighbors for use. The year before last, he went straight to Zhabei and privately牽了 a mule raised by someone and was arrested after being discovered. Because he was still young, he was not investigated in depth and was released back home. As a result, he became more daring. The nearby area all knew that Xiao Gouzi's behavior was improper and had long been suspicious of him. The day before yesterday, the Wang family on Qinglong Bridge celebrated their birthday and specially summoned Jiang Fuchen from Wuxi to their home to chant the scriptures. While he was 복星拜斗, Xiao Gouzi took the opportunity to sneak in and secretly stole a gold ring and a silver hairpin placed on the plate and took the loot to a certain pawnshop on Wangjiajiaozui to pawn them. He pawned the gold ring for seven yuan and then went to the Big World in Beishi to游覧. He caught a glimpse of the machine gun horse gambling game in the venue and entered the game to gamble. In a short while, the seven yuan he brought was completely lost. He did not return to the Wang family until around 12 pm. After the gold ring and silver hairpin were lost, they were anxious. Then someone informed them that Xiao Gouzi had come over and was suspicious. They asked his family members. Xiao Gouzi happened to be not at home. They waited until late at night to see him return and immediately called Gao Xiangzhou, the guard police of the 10th Post in the area, to arrest him and take him to the 1st Sub-Precinct of the管一區 for preliminary interrogation.

Declarations from Various Unions in Zhabei 156

Regarding Assisting the Fengtang Porcelain Union

To the Shanghai newspaper offices and all compatriots in the city: Please be aware that we remember last year on this day, the Shanghai Fengtang Porcelain Factory Union once initiated a labor strike to demand improvements in living conditions and the signing of employment contracts. Unexpectedly, the factory owners, relying on personal connections with the Hong case, used the excuse of a strike to cut off the livelihood of the workers. We and other organizations, located in Zhabei, having heard of this, believe that under party rule, our workers should strive to escape from inhuman living conditions.

As our compatriots at the Fengtang factory face this kind of threat and oppression and appeal for help, how can we stand idly by? Moreover, the success or failure of the Fengtang factory owners’ methods is truly a test for all factory owners in Shanghai. If they succeed in implementing it, others will follow suit, and the entire labor movement in Shanghai will gradually be wiped out. For the sake of others, for our own sake, and for the sake of the future of the revolution, in addition to jointly submitting a petition to the party and government authorities to severely punish the Fengtang factory owners, we also hope that all workers and compatriots from all walks of life in Shanghai will extend their sympathy and assistance. This is not only the fortune of the Fengtang Union but also the fortune of the entire Shanghai labor movement. This is our declaration.

The Entire Committee of the Commercial Press Union, The Staff and Workers Union of the General Affairs Department of the Commercial Press, The Staff and Workers Union of the Compilation and Translation Department of the Commercial Press, The Staff and Workers Union of the Distribution Department of the Commercial Press, The British-Owned Water and Fire Company Union, The Huazhuang Binding Zhabei District Union, The Renhe Cigar Factory Union, The Yongtai Cigar Factory Union, The Jingyi Leather Factory Union, The Pig Bristle Union, The Organ Industry Union, The Mirror Wood Union, The Tattoo Workers Union, The China Merchant Public Bus Workers Union, The Preparatory Committee of the Yunfei Automobile Union, The Yifeng Porcelain Factory Union, The Coal and Firewood Industry Union, The Qingde Rubber Factory Union, The Seventh Silk Factory Workers Union, The Eighth Silk Factory Workers Union, The Tiancheng Silk Weaving Union, The Auto Painting Union, The Sino-Foreign Printing Union, and more than thirty other unions.

County Magistrate Yan's Report on Budget Preparation 157

At the Shanghai County Government's weekly memorial service this morning, County Magistrate Yan reported on the preparation of the 19th year's budget, saying that today is June 30th, the end of the 18th year, and tomorrow is July 1st, the beginning of the 19th year. The things the local government should do in the future all depend on whether the 19th year's budget can be prepared and finalized. If the budget cannot be finalized, the progress of various undertakings will face difficulties. Therefore, the county government has paid great attention to the preparation of the 19th year's budget. First, it notified all county-affiliated agencies to submit their budget proposals to the county for compilation before June 15th. Subsequently, the county-affiliated agencies submitted their budgets one after another. After review, it was found that the County Education Bureau had more income, and the budget could barely be established. The Construction Bureau had a slight surplus in the 18th year, but starting from the 19th year, the provincial subsidies were canceled, and the administrative expenses were felt to be difficult. The surplus funds for undertakings were exhausted, and there were also concerns about future shortages. The public security expenses were originally allocated by the city government, which seemed unrelated to the county funds. However, currently, only half of the allocation has been made, which is still insufficient. It is necessary to reduce administrative expenses and police salaries as much as possible. In addition, the replenishment of clothing and firearms requires funds at any time, and it is difficult to raise them. The current budgets of various districts are insufficient. The first district is relatively better, while the second and third districts and below are very difficult. The expenses of the County Party Headquarters and the Agricultural Field are completely without funding. The county government previously received a request from the director of the County Agricultural Field to reassess the land price in order to levy agricultural improvement donations based on the acreage to allocate to the field's expenses. Therefore, it convened several meetings to discuss the reassessment of the land price. As a result, the proposal of the County Agricultural Field has been rejected. The intention of the county government is to work together to establish the 19th year's budget and bring the Shanghai local government onto the right track. However, the people's capacity to bear it is limited, and the county government has no intention of forcing its passage. However, the representatives of various agencies who participate in the budget meeting must broaden their horizons and consider the entire county, not just the agency they represent, and also consider the agencies that have no funding. No matter how difficult it is, we should strive to prepare the 19th year's budget and ensure that the county administration in the 19th year is a little more advanced than in the 18th year.

Clinic Established in Caojiadu 158

The business community in Caojiadu, West Shanghai, including Li Meiqing, Jin Fuchun, Yu Yuqing, Zhu Zhixian, Yao Yu, etc., considering that there are many factories in the area and poor workers are everywhere, and that epidemics are a concern every summer, established a clinic and medicine dispensary in the Shuiyi Hall in the town to benefit the poor and sick. Now that summer has arrived, the clinic has been re-established at the original site in the hall, and Chinese and Western doctors are invited to take turns providing treatment and administering vaccinations without charge. Prescriptions are also dispensed free of charge. It officially opened yesterday, the 1st.

Exhibition of the White Goose Research Institute 162

The White Goose Painting Research Institute held its fourth exhibition of student works yesterday at its original location on Changchun Road, North Sichuan Road. The institute is a pioneering research organization in China with a rigorous mission and excellent achievements, and it has long received enthusiastic support from people in Shanghai. Therefore, the number of visitors was exceptionally high. In total, there were hundreds of student works, with charcoal, powder, and watercolor paintings by Feng Qiuhen, Zhou Xi, He Zhizhen, etc., being particularly outstanding. The pencil sketches by Zhang Xuefu and Cheng Jie showed the most solid foundation. Recent works by instructors, such as the watercolor paintings by Mr. Chen and Mr. Pan and the oil paintings by Mr. Fang and Mr. Shao, all made new contributions. The original manuscripts displayed by the White Goose Art Publication were especially exquisite and unparalleled. However, the exhibition date is only today and tomorrow due to the urgent start of the institute's summer research course, and it will not be extended. Visitors are welcome, and summer research comrades are being recruited, it is said.
