Scheduled Publication of Xin Nanhui Bao 165

Shao Jingzhi, the director of the Dadong News Agency in this city and a native of Nanhui, recently observed that the area is vast and many incidents occur daily. However, due to transportation limitations, it is difficult to know the truth even between places ten miles apart, which is truly regrettable. Furthermore, many fellow villagers are working in other places and want to know the details of their hometown news, but there is no suitable newspaper to meet their needs, which is also regrettable. As for grand pronouncements and reform plans, they cannot be fully announced. Shao believes that this phenomenon is hindering the development of Nanhui, especially in this era where public opinion represents the will of the people and is a precursor to industrial development. Therefore, he hosted a banquet in Nanhui the other day, inviting people from the Party, government, business, academic, and military circles to organize the Xin Nanhui Bao. Preparations are now complete, and the inaugural issue will be published on the 15th of this month. After that, a large broadsheet will be published every six days. The newspaper is a local newspaper that does not discuss politics and economics. Shao will be in charge, and Zhu Wenyuan has been invited to be the editor-in-chief. The office is temporarily located in Nanhui City. It is said that all newspaper vendors in this city will sell it.

The American Allied Bank, The Underwriters Savings Bank for the Far East Lnc., is a Shanghai-based American organization with a capital of 500,000 yuan, fully paid up in one installment. It is registered in the government of Connecticut, USA, and operates in accordance with a special banking permit, engaging in various businesses such as current and time deposits, loans, and remittances. Starr, is the founder of Allied Life Insurance Company and currently serves as the chairman and general manager. The solid foundation and outstanding reputation of Allied Life Insurance Company are all due to Mr. Starr's efforts. Now, he is transferring his spirit of managing life insurance to the banking business, and its stability and reliability are self-evident. Furthermore, with the assistance of Manager Zhang Shouqing, who has been engaged in banking business for more than ten years and has extensive knowledge and experience, he will be more than capable of handling the position of manager. The bank's main branch is located at No. 17, the Bund, and officially opened on the 5th. The interest rates on deposits are particularly favorable, and the office hours have been extended to facilitate customers.

Record of the Sino-Foreign Rickshaw Merchant Association Meeting 169

The Sino-Foreign Rickshaw Merchant Association of this city convened an emergency meeting yesterday afternoon. The meeting proceeded as usual. The meeting items were: (1) Proposal to set up public tea pavilions. (2) Proposal to distribute Summer Heat Relief Water. (3) Proposal to find ways to maintain business in light of the skyrocketing prices of rubber, hardware, and vehicle materials. (4) Proposal to prepare the iron sheets for the summonses by the association itself. The public unanimously elected Bao Guoxiang as the chairman. He reported to the public on the purpose of the meeting and the matters to be discussed, stating that the association should, as an example, set up more tea pavilions at the entrances of various roads in the summer to provide coolies with tea to drink, and also distribute Summer Heat Relief Water from various companies to provide emergency relief to coolie rickshaw pullers suffering from heatstroke. However, these two proposals have already been implemented, but they must be reported to everyone. Gu Songfa and Xi Yingchuan then spoke in succession, all saying that the current skyrocketing prices of rubber, hardware, vehicle materials, etc., are due to the influence of gold prices, and the meager rickshaw rents collected by the various companies are insufficient to cover costs. The rubber and hardware material industry has also declared price increases. If our fellow members continue to collect rents as before, it will be difficult to make ends meet. If we allow the prices of rubber and hardware vehicle materials to rise without falling, our business losses will be impossible to make up. We should find ways to maintain and subsidize them. After discussion by the members, the only way is to slightly increase the rickshaw rents to subsidize them, otherwise, there is no other way to save this situation. The motion was then passed immediately. Finally, it was agreed that the iron sheets for the summonses on the rickshaws should be handled by the association itself in accordance with Zhu Lawyer's letter, and will be handled after a letter to the Finance Bureau. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Xi Chenshi Asks the Pharmaceutical Industry Association for Assistance 170

Chen, the wife of Xi Shaofeng, the owner of the Xi Changsheng Tang pharmacy in Zhabei, submitted a petition to the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association yesterday, stating: "With tears, the petitioner Xi Chenshi respectfully presents this petition to the executive committee members of the Shanghai National Pharmaceutical Industry Association: The clerk of the store, Luo Xishun, has a habitual addiction and is out all day long. Therefore, he has no accomplishments in the store's work, and after returning to the store, he quarrels with the friends and the store owner. In short, his sins are too numerous to mention. My husband, Shaofeng, has repeatedly wanted to dismiss him, but because he has the union to protect him, he has never been able to do so, causing my husband, Shaofeng, to become depressed and mentally disordered. A few days ago, he went out of his mind and lost his slippers, causing my family to cry and panic. Everyone thought that if there were any accidents, the whole store would be like a ship without a rudder, losing its master, and how would we live in the future? After searching through the newspapers, fortunately, the second branch of the second district of the Public Security Bureau sent him back, but only his breath remained. Currently, he is being treated by a doctor, and he has slightly recovered, but he is still constantly calling for Luo Xishun to harm him. In this situation, I have no choice but to submit this petition to the association for assistance, praying that it will be forwarded to the Social Affairs Bureau and consulted with the union to allow the store to dismiss Luo Xishun so that my husband's heart disease can still be cured with a heart medicine. Otherwise, if my husband becomes more depressed or suffers an accident, not only will my family lose its livelihood, but the livelihoods of the friends in the store will also be unable to be preserved, which is not the way of people's livelihood. In short, if Luo Xishun can be dismissed, it will not only be the good fortune of my family but also the good fortune of the friends, and it will be the good fortune of the people's livelihood of society. I cannot express my hope enough. I respectfully submit this petition, etc." It is heard that the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association has forwarded the petition to the Social Affairs Bureau for review.

The association will first publish an advertisement of thanks and then hold a public banquet to express our gratitude. The resolution was passed. (6) The placement has now been successfully completed, and the support association should be terminated on a regular basis. The 16th of this month was set as the deadline for all procedures to be completed, and all committee members must be convened to the meeting that morning to take a group photo as a memorial. The resolution was passed. (7) Omitted. (8) Omitted. (9) The meeting adjourned.

Weather Report 172

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday stated that the coastal areas and the Yangtze River basin will be hot and cloudy with localized thunderstorms. There will be southeasterly winds over the Yellow Sea and the East China Sea. A hurricane in the Pacific Ocean will turn northwest. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 pm yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 93.4 and the lowest was 78.3. On the same day last year, the highest was 76.8 and the lowest was 72.9.

Letter Received 173

To the esteemed editor: With utmost respect, yesterday I read in your newspaper's local news section a report on the Health Bureau's conscientious epidemic prevention work, in which my company and the Zu'an Company were reprimanded for preventing workers from receiving injections, etc. At the same time, I received a letter from the Health Bureau to my company with the same content. I believe that the Health Bureau's move to protect workers and prevent cholera is beneficial to the working population and protects manufacturers. Manufacturers generally deeply appreciate this and see no need to prevent it. However, the doctor at the time did not follow hygiene procedures, causing a reaction from the workers. After your newspaper published the report, I fear that those who do not know the truth will cause misunderstandings between labor and capital, which is greatly related to the future of the factory. In addition to replying to the Health Bureau with the facts, I am sending the original manuscript to be published, and I would be grateful. I wish you peace and prosperity. From Lin Zhetong, July 6th, with the Xiangya Company's seal.

Attached is the original letter to the Health Bureau: Responding with respect, I have just received your bureau's letter, which states that according to reports, the bureau sent a doctor to your factory on the 2nd of this month to provide free cholera vaccinations to the workers. The workers were about to ask for the vaccinations, but the executives of your factory not only did not enthusiastically supervise and encourage the acceptance of the vaccinations but also added to the obstruction. This unintentional move is nothing more than thinking that the workers' vaccinations will inevitably cost one or two minutes of work time. It can be seen that your factory values private profits more than workers' health, and your vision is short-sighted and your love for the community is weak, which is regrettable. Now, we will still send doctors to your factory to provide free cholera vaccinations to the workers. We hope that the executives of your factory can accept good advice and not obstruct the workers from enjoying the benefits of free prevention. That is the most important thing. After reading this, I was deeply surprised. After the manager was not notified of the doctor sent by your bureau to the factory on July 2, and when the doctor from your bureau arrived at the factory, the factory workers Xu Liangfa, Zhou Debao, and Fang Ermei received the injections. Later, when it came to the pharmacist Huang Zao to start the injections, Huang Zao said that the workers' bodies were mostly unclean and the doctor did not first wipe the skin with alcohol, and the needles used by the doctor were not washed with disinfectant after three injections. He was deeply afraid that he would not be able to prevent cholera but would be infected, so he asked the doctor to disinfect according to hygiene laws before injecting. The doctor did not allow it, so he stopped. I think that the original intention of your bureau chief in sending personnel to give injections was to prevent cholera and benefit the people. However, if the needles used by the doctor were not disinfected at all, the savior would be harming people. It both betrays your bureau chief's love for workers and love for the community and cannot match the trust of the workers in their lives. The doctor did not blame himself for his negligence but added the crime of disregarding workers' health, short-sightedness, and lack of love for the community to the factory executives. I don't know that the factory executives' request for the doctor to disinfect is to protect the workers' lives and show love for the community. The former by letter responded to the correspondence and asked for a change to inform your doctor must follow hygienic laws when performing injections and disinfect the tools and skin at the time of the injection to prevent infection. This pays respect to the Shanghai City Health Bureau Chief.

Shanghai Market

Market News 174

Yan Hua Lou Restaurant, located across from Dan Gui Stage No. 1 on Fourth Avenue, declares that this restaurant always selects the finest vegetarian dishes every summer to serve its patrons. As summer is approaching again this year, this restaurant is paying even greater attention than last year. It has specially hired a Buddhist master from Guangdong's Tianchan Temple to oversee the cooking. The master arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, bringing with him various vegetarian ingredients and seasonings produced in Guangdong. The cooking methods are exquisite, the flavors are suitable for all tastes, and the dishes are novel and unique. Therefore, recently, people from all walks of life have been flocking to enjoy vegetarian meals, all praising that they are indeed of high quality and low price. In addition, more than a thousand cups of freshly made pure vegetarian five-spice fermented bean curd have arrived. This fermented bean curd can stimulate the appetite and aid digestion, making it an excellent side dish for summer meals. A large cup costs 50 cents, and a small cup costs 25 cents.

Qihua Company on Nanjing Road declares that its piece goods department is currently having a truly great summer sale. In particular, true silk "Hua Er Sha" is priced from one yuan to one yuan and fifty-eight cents per foot. Figured linen is priced at four yards per yuan, non-refundable. Figured cloth is priced at six yards per yuan. An inexpensive clothing material section has also been established, with "Hua Er Sha" cheongsam material priced from 80 cents to one yuan per piece. Silk thread openwork gauze cheongsam material is priced at one yuan and fifty cents per piece. "Hua Er Chou" cheongsam material is priced at one yuan and fifty cents per piece. Figured fu silk cheongsam material is priced at one yuan and fifty cents per piece.

The Continental Hotel at the San Mao Ge Bridge on Avenue Edward VII declares that since its opening, business has been exceptionally prosperous. At this time of hot weather, the number of guests has increased even more. There is concern that the elevator going up and down may be dangerous. This hotel, at great expense, has purchased a brand new elevator mechanism from Germany. Workers are being hired to remove all the old mechanisms and install the new ones as soon as possible, and insurance devices are being added to ensure the safety of passengers and promote business development. It is scheduled to resume normal operation on the 12th.

The Green Bus Company at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Hongjiang Road declares that it is celebrating its first anniversary since opening. To commemorate this occasion, it has specially prepared five thousand silk handkerchiefs. Starting from the 7th of this month, they will be respectfully presented to everyone to thank them for their patronage over the years. The gifts will be given away while supplies last. The company's telephone numbers are 41188 and 45222.

Lianyi Trading Company, next door to the Universal Theater on East Seward Road in Hongkou, declares that in order to better serve its customers, it is offering Lianyi stationery and notebooks, which it manufactures, at the original price. Customers who purchase two yuan worth of these two items will also receive a compilation of famous novels or everyday necessities as a gift. Since the promotion began, sales at the store have been exceptionally brisk, and mail orders from other places have been flooding in. Customers have all expressed satisfaction.

Jiufu Company on Buck Road declares that the Sheng Dan it produces uses carefully selected ingredients and promotes national products. It is an essential summer health product, and since its release, it has become widely popular and is an essential item for those with health awareness. In order to promote summer health among all workers, this company has specially prepared sample packages of Sheng Dan to be given away at famous national product factories. Many have already been given away, and recently, a large batch was prepared to be given away at the Shenxin No. 2 Textile Factory on Yichang Road and the Shenxin No. 5 Textile Factory at Gao Lang Bridge.

Theater News 175

Youlian Film Company declares that after the release of the first and second installments of "Wild River Heroine," business has been exceptionally good. The third, fourth, and fifth installments have also been filmed and are expected to be edited and completed in a month, after which they will be shown on the screen again. In addition, the first team, directed by Chen Kengran, is currently preparing an emotionally resonant and richly expressive drama titled "Consort Yu." The plot is subtle and tortuous, and when it is released, it will surely make the audience both laugh and cry, with their emotions stirred. The second team, directed by Wen Yi and Wen Min and starring Fan Peng, has also begun filming the fourth and fifth installments of "Children Heroes."

The Golden Grand Theater declares that "The Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse," which is being screened at this theater, is a meticulously crafted work by the world's greatest director, Rex Ingram, starring a cast of great names including Janet Gaynor, Mary Duncan, and Nancy D'Este. Today is the last day this film will be screened at this theater. Starting tomorrow, it will be replaced by "Four Sons," a recent masterpiece by director John Ford, along with the comedy "The Old Bachelor."
